)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* *FILE                       - A MODE 4 TYPE DO
)@@G@@FILE SGS IS    *******  @H@@@@. *******                             -   DP

)@@G@@EPEAT LAST' FOLLOWS AN '*IF LAST ....' STATEMENT,  *******  @H@@@@. ****DS
)@@G@@*** THE STATEMENT BEFORE THE '*IF' STATEMENT IS REPEATED UNTIL *******  DT
)@@G@@@H@@@@. ******* THE CONDITION ON THE '*IF' STATEMENT BECOMES TRUE.      DU

)@@G@@AT SGS IMAGE   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IS REPEATED UNTIL A RESPONSE OF DW
)@@G@@'$END' IS GIVEN.           *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DX

)@@G@@R OF '$SKIP' TO ANY SGS QUESTION, WILL SKIP        *******  @H@@@@. ****DZ

)@@G@@TO INPUT LETTER*******  @H@@@Q. ********                                KS

)@@G@@                           *******  @H@9@8. *******       'TIME' IS STARON
)@@G@@T TIME OF SEARCH (TDATE$)              *******  @H@9@8. *******       'WOO
)@@G@@D #' IS WORD NO. IN BUFFER WHICH IS TO             *******  @H@9@8. ****OP
)@@G@@***              BE USED AS A SEARCH KEY                       *******  OQ
)@@G@@@H@9@8. *******       'KEY'  IS KEY TO BE USED                          OR
)@@G@@   *******  @H@9@8. *******       'BUFFER' IS OUTPUT BUFFER             OS
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. *******                                 OT
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@9@8. ******* 'BUFFER' = 0 IF LOG OU
)@@G@@FINISHED OR ERROR                      *******  @H@@@9. ******* 'BUFFER'OV
)@@G@@ = 0 IF LOG FINISHED OR ERROR.                     *******  @H@@@9. ****OW
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  OX
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ******* WHENEVER A NEW BLOCK IS READ, THE EXTERNAL TAG 'NEWBLOCKOY
)@@G@@'  *******  @H@@@8. ******* WILL = 1.                                   OZ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. *******                                 PA
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@9. ******* IF USER WISHES TO SKPB
)@@G@@IP REST OF CURRENT BLOCK, THE EXTERNAL *******  @H@@@9. ******* 'ENTRYNUPC
)@@G@@M' SHOULD BE SET TO 0.                             *******  @H@@@9. ****PD
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  PE
)@@G@@@H@@@9. ******* IF A FILE NAMED 'LOG$' IS ASSIGNED TO RUN, SUBROUTINE   PF
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. ******* WILL READ THAT FILE RATHER THAN CURRENT SYSTPG
)@@G@@EM MASTER LOG  *******  @H@@@9. ******* FILE ON MASS STORAGE.           PH
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. *******                     PI
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@9. ******* IF EXTERPJ
)@@G@@NAL TAG 'PRINTCYCLE' IS SET, A SUMMARY             *******  @H@@@9. ****PK
)@@G@@*** LINE IS PRINTED FOR EACH CYCLE OF THE SYSTEM MASTER LOG    *******  PL
)@@G@@@H@@@9. ******* FILE SCANNED.                                           PM
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. *******                                             PN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. ******* COUNTS OF THE NUMBER OF BLOCKS APO
)@@G@@ND THE NUMBER OF RECORDS   *******  @H@@@9. ******* ARE MAINTAINED IN EXPP
)@@G@@TERNAL TAGS 'NBLOCKS' AND 'NRECS'.     *******  @H@@@9. *******         PQ
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****PR
)@@G@@*** THIS SUBROUTINE IS COMPATIBLE WITH FORTRAN V AND           *******  PS
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ******* ASCII FORTRAN.                                          PT
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. *******                                             PU
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. ******* THE 'BYTESUB' SUBROUTINES ARE REPV
)@@G@@FERENCED.                  *******  @H@@@9. *******                     PW
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* REVISIONPX
)@@G@@ SUMMARY                                           *******  @H@@@8. ****PY
)@@G@@*** ----------------                                           *******  PZ
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         QA
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R1  - FIRST RELEASE                        QB
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R2  - REMOVE TAPE LOGIC AND REPQC
)@@G@@LACE WITH                  *******  @H@@@8. *******      - CHECK FOR PREQD
)@@G@@-ASSIGNED LOG FILES                    *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R3  - AQE
)@@G@@SSUME BLOCKS SPAN LESS THAN 1 HOUR OF DATA         *******  @H@@@8. ****QF
)@@G@@***      - SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO ENTRIES                         *******  QG
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******      - ALLOW MULTI-REEL LOG TAPES                       QH
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. *******      - SIGNAL CALLING PROG WHEN NEW BLOCK REQI
)@@G@@AD             *******  @H@@@8. *******      - DON'T LEAVE ANY MASS STORQJ
)@@G@@AGE LOG FILES ASSIGNED     *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R4  - SKIP EXEC 8 EQK
)@@G@@NTRIES UNLESS PRIVILEGED               *******  @H@@@9. *******      - AQL
)@@G@@SSEMBLE WITH MASM                                  *******  @H@@@9. ****QM
)@@G@@*** 1R5  - CHECK FOR AN ALTERNATE LOG FILE CALLED 'LOG$'       *******  QN
)@@G@@@H@@@9. *******      - CALCULATE SECTOR ADDRESS OF 1ST BLOCK TO ALLOW   QO
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. *******        FOR FILES COPIED FROM TAPE           QP
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. *******      - ASSIGN SYSTEM LOG FILES WQQ
)@@G@@ITH 'I' OPTION             *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R6  - FIX LOGIC FORQR
)@@G@@ SEARCH KEY OPTION                     *******  @H@@@9. *******      - AQS
)@@G@@DD 'L' OPTION SUMMARY                              *******  @H@@@9. ****QT
)@@G@@***      - ADD STRING SCAN FEATURE                             *******  QU
)@@G@@@H@@@9. *******      - CALCULATE 1ST CYCLE OF LOG FILE                  QV
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R7  - EXTERNALIZE TAG 'ENTRYNUM' FOR SKIPPIQW
)@@G@@NG BLOCK       *******  @H@@@9. *******      - EXTERNALIZE TAG 'PRINTCYCQX
)@@G@@LE' FOR CYCLE SUMMARY      *******  @H@@@9. ******* 1R8  - ADD EXTERNAL QY
)@@G@@CELLS 'NBLOCKS' & 'NRECS'              *******  @H@@@9. *******      - UQZ
)@@G@@SE 1180 INSTRUCTIONS                               *******  @H@@@9. ****RA
)@@G@@*** 1R9  - FIX LATEST CYCLE BUG                                *******  RB
)@@G@@@H@@@'. ******* 1R10 - ADD LOOK AHEAD CYCLE FEATURE                     RC
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. *******                                             RD
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************RE
)@@G@@**********************************  @#@9@8          AXR$    @]@9@8$(1),RRF
)@@G@@EADLG*@#@@@9$(1),READLG* AXR$ @H@@@8          L         X10,X11         RG
)@@G@@  . GET PARAMETER TABLE (IN X11 IF FOR V  @E@@@8          TZ,S1     0,X1RH
)@@G@@1             .   , IN A0 IF FTN)   @ @@@8          L         X10,A0    RI
)@@G@@@^@@@8          SZ        BUFF@ @@@8          L         X5,POINTER@E@@@8RJ
)@@G@@          TZ        FIRST             . FIRST TIME ENTERED? @B@9@8      RK
)@@G@@    J         CONT1             . NO@B@@@9          J         CONT2     RL
)@@G@@        . NO@F@9@8          S         X10,FIRST         . YES, SET FIRSTRM
)@@G@@ TIME KEY   @F@@@9          SP1       FIRST             . YES, SET FIRSTRN
)@@G@@ TIME KEY   @E@@@9          PCT$      BUFFER,5          . GET PART OF PCRO
)@@G@@T     @F@@@9          L,S2      A0,BUFFER+4       . IF RUN PRIVILEGED, SRP
)@@G@@ET KEY@ @@@9          TEP,U     A0,040    @^@@@9          SP1       PRIVRQ
)@@G@@@G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE1         . '@USE MASTER,SYS$*SYSTEM$LRR
)@@G@@OG$'  @H@@@8          FACIL$    FACPKT            . IS THERE A LOG FILE RS
)@@G@@ASSIGNED ALREADY? @F@@@8          TNZ,S1    FACPKT+6          . IF FILE RT
)@@G@@NOT PRE-ASSIGNED, @H@9@8          J         CONT0             .     GO TRU
)@@G@@O REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @H@/@9          J         CONT0           RV
)@@G@@  .     GO TO REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @H@@@/          J         CONTRW
)@@G@@1             .     GO TO REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @F@9@8          S RX
)@@G@@        A0,PREASG         . FILE PRE-ASSIGNED, SET KEY@F@@@9          SPRY
)@@G@@1       PREASG            . FILE PRE-ASSIGNED, SET KEY@F@9@8          J RZ
)@@G@@        CONT1             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIC     @F@@@9          J SA
)@@G@@        CONT2             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIC     @E@;@9CONT0     E$SB
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@;@9          E$MSG   SC
)@@G@@  USE @D@;@9          E$DECV    0,,U              . PRESENT CYCLE @#@;@9SD
)@@G@@          E$MSGR  @G@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . '@USE LOSE
)@@G@@G$,SYS$*SYSTEM$LOG$(0)' @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . '@SF
)@@G@@ASG,AI LOG$'@F@/@;CONT0     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST SG
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @F@@@/CONT1     SZ        A5                . ASSIGN LATEST SH
)@@G@@LOG CYCLE   @ @@@;          L,U       A6,' '    @ @@@;          SLJ     SI
)@@G@@  CYCLE     @D@@@9          MSCON$    MSCONPKT          . GET LEAD ITEM SJ
)@@G@@@H@@@9                                      . CHANGE MSCON PKT TO READ MSK
)@@G@@AIN ITEM    @E@@@9          SP1,S3    MSCONPKT+3        .   FOR LATER CASL
)@@G@@LLS   @G@@@9          L,S4      A0,BUFFER+9       . CALCULATE OLDEST RELSM
)@@G@@ CYCLE-1    @^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@C@@@9          SN        A0,LSN
)@@G@@OGCYCLE       . STORE   @E@9@8CONT0     LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GESO
)@@G@@T NEXT LOG CYCLE  @E@/@9CONT1     LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXTSP
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@/          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CSQ
)@@G@@YCLE  @C@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR   @F@9@8CONT1 SR
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,READ          . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@9CONT2 SS
)@@G@@    LMJ       X9,READ           . READ NEXT MASTER LOG BLOCK@F@@@8      ST
)@@G@@    L         A0,0,X5           . CHECK FOR END OF CYCLE    @ @@@8      SU
)@@G@@    TNE       A0,(-0)   @C@9@8          J         CONT7             . YESV
)@@G@@S     @C@@@9          J         CONT11            . YES     @H@@@8      SW
)@@G@@    TE        A0,SENTINEL       . CHECK FOR LAST TAPE BLOCK SENTINEL    SX
)@@G@@@^@@@8          J         $+3 @G@9@8          SZ        FIRST           SY
)@@G@@  . INITIALIZE FIRST TIME THRU FLAG @F@@@9          SZ        FIRST     SZ
)@@G@@        . CLEAR FIRST TIME THRU FLAG@D@@@8          J         EXIT      TA
)@@G@@        . END OF TAPE   @G@@@8          L         A0,STIME          . CHTB
)@@G@@ECK STARTING TIME IF SPECIFIED@ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT2  @ @@@9TC
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,CONT3  @D@@@8          L         A1,LLOGT        TD
)@@G@@  . GET LOG TIME  @E@@@8          SLJ       DTDATE            . COMPARE TE
)@@G@@WITH STIME  @G@9@8          AU        A2,60*60          . IF STIME MORE TF
)@@G@@THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@9          AU,U      A2,60*60          . IF STIMETG
)@@G@@ MORE THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@8          TP        A3                .   TH
)@@G@@FUTURE, SKIP REST OF BLOCK    @G@9@8          SZ        NBUF            TI
)@@G@@  . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  TJ
)@@G@@        . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @F@9@8          JN        A2,CTK
)@@G@@ONT1          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @F@@@9          JN        A2,CTL
)@@G@@ONT2          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @E@@@9CONT3     TZ        PRIVTM
)@@G@@              . IS RUN PRIVILEGED?  @C@@@9          J         CONT4     TN
)@@G@@        . YES     @F@@@9          L         A0,('EXEC 8')     . NO, SKIPTO
)@@G@@ EXEC 8 ENTRIES   @ @@@9          TNE       A0,LRUNID @ @@@9          J TP
)@@G@@        CONT2     @F@9@8CONT2     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUTQ
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @F@@@9CONT4     L         A0,RUNID          . CHECK RUTR
)@@G@@NID IF SPECIFIED, @G@9@8          JZ        A0,CONT4          .    IGNORTS
)@@G@@ING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @G@@@9          JZ        A0,CONT7          .   TT
)@@G@@ IGNORING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @^@@@8          L,U       X4,5@ @9@8CONT2ATU
)@@G@@    EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@9CONT5     EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@8      TV
)@@G@@    TNE,U     A0,'-'    @ @9@8          J         CONT3     @ @@@9      TW
)@@G@@    J         CONT6     @ @@@8          EX        TEST,X4   @ @9@8      TX
)@@G@@    J         CONT3     @ @@@9          J         CONT6     @^@9@8      TY
)@@G@@    SZ        NBUF@ @@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  @ @9@8          J TZ
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @ @9@8CONT3     JGUA
)@@G@@D       X4,CONT2A @ @@@9CONT6     JGD       X4,CONT5  @F@9@8CONT4     L UB
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @F@@@9CONT7     L UC
)@@G@@        A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          L,UD
)@@G@@H2      A0,0,A1   @F@@@8          TNZ,H1    0,X10             . CHECK IFUE
)@@G@@ TYPE TABLE INPUT @E@9@8          J         CONT4A            . NO, JUSTUF
)@@G@@ ONE TYPE   @E@@@9          J         CONT8             . NO, JUST ONE TUG
)@@G@@YPE   @F@@@8          L,H1      R1,0,X10          . SCAN TYPE TABLE FOR UH
)@@G@@MATCH @ @@@8          L         X1,0,X10  @^@@@8          LXI,U     X1,1UI
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,LTYPE  @ @@@8          SE,H2     A0,0,*X1  UJ
)@@G@@@E@9@8          J         CONT1             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @E@@@9UK
)@@G@@          J         CONT2             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@9@8      UL
)@@G@@    J         CONT5             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @F@@@9      UM
)@@G@@    J         CONT9             . TYPE MATCHES, PROCESS     @E@9@8CONT4AUN
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT5          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @E@@@9CONT8     JZUO
)@@G@@        A0,CONT9          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   @ @@@8          TE      UP
)@@G@@  A0,LTYPE  @ @9@8          J         CONT1     @ @@@9          J       UQ
)@@G@@  CONT2     @G@9@8CONT5     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEARCH KUR
)@@G@@EY IF SPECIFIED   @G@@@9CONT9     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEUS
)@@G@@ARCH KEY IF SPECIFIED   @ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT6  @ @@@9      UT
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT10 @D@@@9          TZ        WDNO              . ISUU
)@@G@@ WORD # = 0?@G@@@9          J         CONT9A            . NO, PLAIN SEARUV
)@@G@@CH KEY SPECIFIED  @G@@@9          L         X1,X5             . YES, STRUW
)@@G@@ING SEARCH SPECIFIED    @ @@@9          L,H2      X2,3,X10  @ @@@9      UX
)@@G@@    L,U       A1,24*6   @^@@@9          L,U       A2,6@A@@@9          LMUY
)@@G@@J       X11,FINDFIELD   @E@@@9          J         CONT2             . NOUZ
)@@G@@ FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@@@9          J         CONT10            . STRING FVA
)@@G@@OUND, CONTINUE    @ @9@8          L         X4,WDNO   @ @@@9CONT9A    L VB
)@@G@@        X4,WDNO   @ @@@8          A         X4,X5     @ @@@8          L VC
)@@G@@        A1,0,X4   @ @@@8          TE        A1,A0     @ @9@8          J VD
)@@G@@        CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @F@9@8CONT6     L,VE
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@F@@@9CONT10    L,VF
)@@G@@U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'S AREA@ @@@8          L,VG
)@@G@@U       X4,BUFF   @^@@@8          LXI,U     X4,1@ @@@8          L       VH
)@@G@@  X6,X5     @^@@@8          LXI,U     X6,1@ @@@8          BT        X4,0VI
)@@G@@,*X6  @E@@@8          S         X5,POINTER        . SAME BLOCK POINTER  VJ
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         EXIT              . RETURN  @I@9@8CONT7     TNVK
)@@G@@Z       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FILE, FINISHED     VL
)@@G@@@I@@@9CONT11    TNZ       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FVM
)@@G@@ILE, FINISHED     @E@9@8          LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GET NEXTVN
)@@G@@ LOG CYCLE  @E@@@9          LMJ       X9,NEXT           . GET NEXT LOG CVO
)@@G@@YCLE  @H@@@8          J         EXIT              . ERROR - FINISHED SEAVP
)@@G@@RCH (NO FIND)     @C@9@8          J         CONT1             . CONTINUEVQ
)@@G@@@C@@@9          J         CONT2             . CONTINUE@F@@@8EXIT      TZVR
)@@G@@,S1     0,X10             . CHECK FOR FOR V OR FTN    @C@@@8          J VS
)@@G@@        0,X10             . FTN     @C@@@8          J         6,X10     VT
)@@G@@        . FOR V   @[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. **********************************VU
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@8. *******              RVV
)@@G@@EAD LOG ENTRY SUBROUTINE                     *******  @H@@@8. **********VW
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @[@@@8VX
)@@G@@.     @]@@@8READ      . @F@9@8          TZ        NBUF              . ISVY
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @F@@@9          TZ        ENTRYNUM          . ISVZ
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @B@@@8          J         READ3             . NOWA
)@@G@@@I@@@8          L         A0,READP+5        . YES, INCREMENT DRUM ADDRESWB
)@@G@@S BY 8 SECTORS    @^@@@8          A,U       A0,8@ @@@8READ1     S       WC
)@@G@@  A0,READP+5@F@@@8          IOW$      READP             . READ NEXT 224 WD
)@@G@@WORD BLOCK  @ @@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3   @C@@@8          J       WE
)@@G@@  READE             . ERROR   @F@@@9          INC       NBLOCKS         WF
)@@G@@  . INCREMENT BLOCK COUNT     @#@@@9          NOP     @E@@@8          L WG
)@@G@@        A0,('SYSLOG')     . LOG FILE HEADER ?   @ @@@8          TE      WH
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @B@@@8          J         READ2             . NO@G@@@8      WI
)@@G@@    L         A0,BUFFER+2       . YES, GET SECTOR ADDRESS OF DATA @G@@@9WJ
)@@G@@          A         A0,READP+5        . ADD TO PRESENT SECTOR ADDRESS   WK
)@@G@@@G@@@8          J         READ1             . GO BACK AND READ THAT SECTWL
)@@G@@OR    @F@@@8READ2     L,S6      A0,BUFFER         . SET MAX NO. OF BUFFEWM
)@@G@@RS    @G@@@8          JZ        A0,READ           . SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO WN
)@@G@@ENTRIES     @ @@@8          S         A0,MNBUF  @F@9@8          L,U     WO
)@@G@@  A0,1              . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@F@@@9          SP1     WP
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@A@9@8          S       WQ
)@@G@@  A0,NEWBLOCK     @^@@@8          J         $+2 @G@@@8READ3     SZ      WR
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . CLEAR NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG    @F@9@8          L WS
)@@G@@        A0,NBUF           . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @F@@@9          L WT
)@@G@@        A0,ENTRYNUM       . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @^@@@8          AUWU
)@@G@@,U      A0,1@ @@@8          MSI,U     A0,28     @ @@@8          A,U     WV
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @ @@@8          S         A0,X5     @F@@@8          TG      WW
)@@G@@  A1,MNBUF          . IF = MNBUF, RESET TO 0    @^@@@8          SZ      WX
)@@G@@  A1  @ @9@8          S         A1,NBUF   @A@@@9          S         A1,EWY
)@@G@@NTRYNUM     @C@9@8          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @F@@@9WZ
)@@G@@          INC       NRECS             . INCREMENT NO. OF RECORDS  @#@@@9XA
)@@G@@          NOP     @C@@@9          J         0,X9              . RETURN  XB
)@@G@@@F@@@8READE     .                           . CLEAN END-OF-FILE CHECK   XC
)@@G@@@E@@@8          L,S1      A0,READP+3        . CHECK FOR 1ST EOF   @^@@@8XD
)@@G@@          TE,U      A0,1@F@@@8          J         EXIT              . NOXE
)@@G@@T EOF, OTHER I/O ERROR  @E@@@8          IOW$      READP             . REXF
)@@G@@AD NEXT RECORD    @D@@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3           . I/O ERROXG
)@@G@@R?    @F@@@8          J         EXIT              . YES, PROBABLY DOUBLEXH
)@@G@@ EOF  @F@@@8          L,H2      A0,READP+3        . CHECK IF 14 WD BUFFEXI
)@@G@@R READ@ @@@8          TE,U      A0,14     @E@@@8          J         EXITXJ
)@@G@@              . NO, GARBAGE READ    @G@@@8          L         A0,(054160XK
)@@G@@0000000) . CHECK FOR END-OF-TAPE SDF LABEL@ @@@8          TE        A0,BXL
)@@G@@UFFER @E@@@8          J         EXIT              . NO, GARBAGE READ    XM
)@@G@@@G@@@8          TSWAP$    FACPKT            . CLEAN END-OF-REEL, SWAP TAXN
)@@G@@PES   @^@@@8          J         READ@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************XO
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@8. ****XP
)@@G@@******           GET NEXT LOG CYCLE SUBROUTINE                 *******  XQ
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************XR
)@@G@@**********  @[@@@8.     @]@@@8NEXT      . @D@9@8          CSF$      FREEXS
)@@G@@,NFREE        . @FREE MASTER  @D@@@9          CSF$      FREE,NFREE      XT
)@@G@@  . @FREE LOG$    @E@9@8          L,S3      A1,CYCLE          . IS CYCLEXU
)@@G@@ = -0 ?     @E@@@9NEXTA     INC       LOGCYCLE          . INCREMENT LOGCXV
)@@G@@YCLE  @D@9@8NEXTA     TNE,U     A1,'0'            . IF SO, ERROR  @F@@@9XW
)@@G@@          J         0,X9              . IF LOGCYCLE WAS 0, ERROR  @ @9@8XX
)@@G@@          J         0,X11     @D@9@8          AN,U      A1,1            XY
)@@G@@  . UPDATE CYCLE  @ @9@8          S,S3      A1,CYCLE  @E@'@9          E$XZ
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@'@9          E$MSG   YA
)@@G@@  USE @A@'@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     @A@@@'          L       YB
)@@G@@  A5,LOGCYCLE     @^@'@9          A,U       A0,1@^@@@'          A,U     YC
)@@G@@  A5,1@ @@@'          L,U       A6,' '    @E@@@'          SLJ       CYCLYD
)@@G@@E             . ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE   @#@;@9          E$DECV  @#@;@9      YE
)@@G@@    E$MSGR  @G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE          . @USE MASTER,SYYF
)@@G@@S$*SYSTEM$...     @F@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . @USE LOGYG
)@@G@@$,SYS$*SYSTEM$... @D@9@8          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A MYH
)@@G@@ASTER @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A LOG$   @E@@@8YI
)@@G@@          JN        A0,NEXTA          . NG, TRY NEXT CYCLE  @H@@@9      YJ
)@@G@@    TNZ       PRINTCYCLE        . DOES USER WANT MASTER LOG SUMMARY?    YK
)@@G@@@B@@@9          J         NEXTB             . NO@G@@@9          MSCON$  YL
)@@G@@  MSCONPKT          . YES, GET MAIN ITEM FOR LOG FILE @E@@@9          E$YM
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . INITIATE EDITOR     @D@@@9          E$FD2   YN
)@@G@@  BUFFER+1          . QUALIFIER     @^@@@9          E$CHAR    '*' @D@@@9YO
)@@G@@          E$FD2     BUFFER+3          . FILE-NAME     @^@@@9          E$YP
)@@G@@CHAR    '(' @D@@@9          E$DECV    BUFFER+17,,T3     . ABS CYCLE     YQ
)@@G@@@^@@@9          E$MSG     MESS@A@@@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     YR
)@@G@@@^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@D@@@9          E$DECV                    YS
)@@G@@  . REL CYCLE     @#@@@9          E$MSGR  @E@@@9          E$DAY3    BUFFYT
)@@G@@ER+19         . CATALOGUE TDATE     @^@@@9          E$SKIP    1   @ @@@9YU
)@@G@@          E$TIME    BUFFER+19 @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1           YV
)@@G@@  . SKIP A LINE   @E@@@9          E$PRINT                     . PRINT SUYW
)@@G@@MMARY LINE  @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   YX
)@@G@@@G@@@'NEXTB     TNZ       STIME             . WAS A START TIME SPECIFIEDYY
)@@G@@?     @B@;@'          J         NEXTX             . NO@B@@@;          J YZ
)@@G@@        NEXTC             . NO@F@@@'          A,U       A5,1            ZA
)@@G@@  . YES, ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE +1 @E@@@'          L,U       A6,'1'          ZB
)@@G@@  .   FOR LOOK AHEAD    @ @@@'          SLJ       CYCLE     @H@@@'      ZC
)@@G@@    JN        A0,NEXTC          . PROBLEM WITH THAT CYCLE, FORGET IT    ZD
)@@G@@@F@@@'          MSCON$    MSCONPKT1         . GET MAIN ITEM OF CYCLE    ZE
)@@G@@@G@@@'          L         A0,STIME          . COMPARE START TIME WITH CYZF
)@@G@@CLE'S @E@@@'          L         A1,BUFFER+19      .    CATALOGUE TIME   ZG
)@@G@@@H@@@'          SLJ       DTDATE            . IF START TIME > CATALOGUE ZH
)@@G@@TIME, SKIP  @E@;@'          JN        A2,NEXTA          .    PRESENT CYCZI
)@@G@@LE    @E@@@;          JN        A2,NEXT           .    PRESENT CYCLE    ZJ
)@@G@@@F@9@8          LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZK
)@@G@@@F@'@9NEXTB     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZL
)@@G@@@F@@@'NEXTC     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZM
)@@G@@@ @@@8          S         A0,READP+5@G@9@8          SZ        NBUF      ZN
)@@G@@        . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRZO
)@@G@@YNUM          . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @C@9@8          J       ZP
)@@G@@  1,X11             . RETURN  @C@@@9          J         1,X9            ZQ
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@'/.    @H@@@'. ****************************************ZR
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@'. ******* ASSIGN LOG CYCLE SUBZS
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                *******  @H@@@'. *******         ZT
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@'. ****ZU
)@@G@@*** INPUTS: A5 = REL CYCLE                                     *******  ZV
)@@G@@@H@@@'. *******         A6 = LOG$ SUFFIX                                ZW
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@'. *******                                             ZX
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@'. ****************************************ZY
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@'CYCLE     +         0   @E@@@'ZZ
)@@G@@          E$DIT     EPKT              . EDIT 'USE' IMAGE    @D@@@'      AA
)@@G@@    E$MSG     USE               . '@USE LOG$&'  @D@@@'          E$FD1   AB
)@@G@@  A6                . LOG$ SUFFIX   @C@@@'          E$MSGR              AC
)@@G@@        . ',(&'   @D@@@'          E$DECV    A5                . REL CYCLAD
)@@G@@E     @ @@@'          E$MSGR    . ')'     @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFAE
)@@G@@ER+28,14      . SUBMIT USE IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$DIT     EPKT      AF
)@@G@@        . EDIT 'ASG' IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$MSG     ASG             AG
)@@G@@  . '@ASG,AI LOG$&'     @D@@@'          E$FD1     A6                . LOAH
)@@G@@G$ SUFFIX   @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . SUBMIT ASG IMAAI
)@@G@@GE    @C@@@'          J         *CYCLE            . RETURN  @[@@@'.     AJ
)@@G@@@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************************************************AK
)@@G@@*********************** @H@@@8. *******                                 AL
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. ******* TDATE TIME DIFFERENCAM
)@@G@@E SUBROUTINE                           *******  @H@@@8. *******         AN
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****AO
)@@G@@*** WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 10/07/77                            *******  AP
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         AQ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* THIS SUBROUTINE WILL CALCULATE THE TIME DIFFAR
)@@G@@ERENCE         *******  @H@@@8. ******* IN SECONDS BETWEEN TWO TIMES EXPAS
)@@G@@RESSED IN 'TDATE$' FORMAT. *******  @H@@@8. *******                     AT
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* INPUTS AAU
)@@G@@RE IN A0 & A1 AND OUTPUT IS IN A2.  A2=A1-A0.      *******  @H@@@8. ****AV
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  AW
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************AX
)@@G@@************@#@@@8$(1)      AXR$    @E@@@8DTDATE*   +         0         AY
)@@G@@        . 'SLJ DTDATE' CALL   @D@@@8          DS        A0,DTDIN        AZ
)@@G@@  . SAVE INPUT    @H@@@8          L,H1      A2,DTDIN          . CHECK IFBA
)@@G@@ MMDDYY SAME FOR BOTH TIMES   @ @@@8          TE,H1     A2,DTDIN+1@D@@@8BB
)@@G@@          J         DTDCON1           . NO, TOO BAD   @F@@@8          L BC
)@@G@@        A2,A1             . YES, EASY CALCULATION     @ @@@8          ANBD
)@@G@@        A2,A0     @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . ALL DONEBE
)@@G@@@G@@@8DTDCON1   SLJ       DTDSUB            . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964BF
)@@G@@, D.P.@E@@@8          S         A0,DTDTEMP        . SAVE CONVERTED TIME BG
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,DTDIN+1@G@@@8          SLJ       DTDSUB    BH
)@@G@@        . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964, D.P.@E@@@8          AN        A0,DBI
)@@G@@TDTEMP        . CALCULATE DIFFERENCE@E@@@8          L         A2,A0     BJ
)@@G@@        . GET OUTPUT READY    @D@@@8          DL        A0,DTDIN        BK
)@@G@@  . RESTORE INPUT @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . DONE    BL
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************BM
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@8. ********* CONVERT TDATE$ TO SECONDS SINCE 1964      BN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************BO
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@8DTDSUB    +         0   @D@@@8BP
)@@G@@          S         A0,DTDTEMP+1      . SAVE INPUT    @^@@@8          SZBQ
)@@G@@        A2  @C@@@8          L,S3      A3,DTDTEMP+1      . YEAR    @ @@@8BR
)@@G@@          JZ        A3,DTDSC1 @^@@@8          AN,U      A3,1@ @@@8      BS
)@@G@@    L         A0,A3     @E@@@8          DI,U      A2,4              . CHBT
)@@G@@ECK FOR LEAP YEARS@^@@@8          A,U       A2,1@A@@@8          MSI,U   BU
)@@G@@  A2,60*60*24     @B@@@8          MSI       A0,(60*60*24*365)     @ @@@8BV
)@@G@@          A         A0,A2     @C@@@8DTDSC1    L,S1      A2,DTDTEMP+1    BW
)@@G@@  . MONTH   @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@A@@@8DTDSC2    A         A0,DBX
)@@G@@TDTAB,A2    @ @@@8          JGD       A2,DTDSC2 @C@@@8          L,S2    BY
)@@G@@  A2,DTDTEMP+1      . DAY     @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@E@@@8      BZ
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A2,60*60*24       . CONVERT TO SECS     @D@@@8          A CA
)@@G@@        A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  @G@@@8          L,S3      A3,DCB
)@@G@@TDTEMP+1       . IF LEAP YEAR AND MONTH>FEB,    @H@@@8          AND,U   CC
)@@G@@  A3,3              .    ADD AN EXTRA DAY TO CALCULATION    @ @@@8      CD
)@@G@@    JNZ       A4,DTDSC3 @A@@@8          L,S1      A3,DTDTEMP+1    @^@@@8CE
)@@G@@          TLE,U     A3,3@ @@@8          J         DTDSC3    @A@@@8      CF
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,60*60*24     @C@@@8DTDSC3    L,H2      A2,DTDTEMP+1    CG
)@@G@@  . SECS    @D@@@8          A         A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  CH
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         *DTDSUB           . RETURN  @C@9@8DTDIN     RECI
)@@G@@S       2                 . INPUT   @C@@@9DTDIN     $RES      2         CJ
)@@G@@        . INPUT   @^@9@8DTDTEMP   RES       2   @^@@@9DTDTEMP   $RES    CK
)@@G@@  2   @^@@@8DTDTAB    +         0   @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*3CL
)@@G@@1     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*28     @A@@@8          +       CM
)@@G@@  60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8      CN
)@@G@@    +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     CO
)@@G@@@A@@@8          +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*6CP
)@@G@@0*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8          + CQ
)@@G@@        60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @[@@@8CR
)@@G@@/.    @H@@@8. **********************************************************CS
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@8. **********           D A T A                  CT
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@8. **********************************CU
)@@G@@****************************************  @[@@@8.     @]@9@8$(0)      . CV
)@@G@@@F@9@8NEWBLOCK* RES       1                 . NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG    CW
)@@G@@@G@9@8NBUF      RES       1                 . NO. OF ENTRIES IN LOG BLOCCX
)@@G@@K     @[@@@9$(0)  @ @/@8PF        FORM      12,6,18   @^@9@8POINTER   RECY
)@@G@@S       1   @^@@@9POINTER   $RES      1   @^@9@8FIRST     RES       1   CZ
)@@G@@@^@@@9FIRST     $RES      1   @ @9@8BUFF      EQUF      *4,X10    @ @@@9DA

)@@G@@BUFFER -8   @C@@@9READP     I$OD      'LOG$',R$ 224,BUFFER -8     @B@9@8DJ
)@@G@@USE       '@USE MASTER,  SYS$*SYSTEM$LOG$'@B@'@9USE       '@USE LOG$,SYSDK

)@@G@@NFREE     $EQU      $-FREE    @D@9@8BUFFER    RES       224             DS
)@@G@@  . LOG BLOCK     @D@@@9BUFFER    $RES      224               . LOG BLOCDT
)@@G@@K     @ @@@8LOAD      L,S1      A0,RUNID  @ @@@8          L,S2      A0,RDU
)@@G@@UNID  @ @@@8          L,S3      A0,RUNID  @ @@@8          L,S4      A0,RDV
)@@G@@UNID  @ @@@8          L,S5      A0,RUNID  @ @@@8          L,S6      A0,RDW
)@@G@@UNID  @ @@@8TEST      TNE,S1    A0,LRUNID @ @@@8          TNE,S2    A0,LDX
)@@G@@RUNID @ @@@8          TNE,S3    A0,LRUNID @ @@@8          TNE,S4    A0,LDY
)@@G@@RUNID @ @@@8          TNE,S5    A0,LRUNID @ @@@8          TNE,S6    A0,LDZ
)@@G@@RUNID @ @9@8LTYPE     EQUF      0,X5,S1   @ @@@9LTYPE     $EQUF     0,X5EA
)@@G@@,S1   @ @9@8LLOGT     EQUF      25,X5     @ @@@9LLOGT     $EQUF     25,XEB
)@@G@@5     @ @9@8LRUNID    EQUF      27,X5     @ @@@9LRUNID    $EQUF     27,XEC
)@@G@@5     @^@9@8FACPKT    'MASTER '     @^@@@9FACPKT    'LOG$   '     @^@9@8ED
)@@G@@          RES       7   @^@@@9          $RES      7   @^@9@8PREASG    REEE
)@@G@@S       1   @^@@@9PREASG    $RES      1   @^@@@9PRIV      $RES      1   EF

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IS FOUND, THE FOLLOWING DATA IMAGES WILL BE FP

)@@G@@FIED (ONE PER DATA CARD FOLLOWING      *******  @H@@@@. ******* THE PROCFS
)@@G@@ESSOR CALL).  AS EACH STRING IS MATCHED, IT IS     *******  @H@@@@. ****FT

)@@G@@**********  @H@@@Q. ******** CHECK XQT OPTION $PROC- ISOLATES BIT CORR. IY
)@@G@@TO INPUT LETTER*******  @H@@@Q. ********                                IZ
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@Q. ******** E.G.  TOPT 'U'    =JA
)@@G@@ AND A0,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       TJB
)@@G@@OPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ****JC
)@@G@@****       AOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)                 *******  JD
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********       AOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000000000040)              JE
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SOPT 'U'    = TOP A0,(000000000040)  JF
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SOPT A2,'U' = TOP A2,(000JG
)@@G@@000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       GOPT 'U'    =JH
)@@G@@ ER OPT$                               *******  @H@@@Q. ********        JI
)@@G@@             AND A0,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ****JJ
)@@G@@**********************************************************************  JK
)@@G@@@#@@@QP         $PROC   @^@@@QTOPT**    $NAME     0   @^@@@QAOPT**    $NJL
)@@G@@AME     0   @^@@@QGOPT**    $NAME     1   @^@@@QSOPT**    $NAME     2   JM
)@@G@@@A@@@Q          $DO P(0,0)=1 , ER OPT$    @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)<2)JN
)@@G@@**(P(1)=1) , AND A0,(1*/('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)=0)JO
)@@G@@**(P(1)>1) , AND P(1,1),(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)=2)JP
)@@G@@**(P(1)=1) , TOP A0,(1*/('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)=2)JQ
)@@G@@**(P(1)>1) , TOP P(1,1),(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@QJR
)@@G@@.     @H@@@Q. **********************************************************JS
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@Q. ******** FORTRAN CALL $PROC                   JT
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. ********                          JU
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ******** CALL SUBR A,BJV
)@@G@@,C,D  = LMJ X11,SUBR                         *******  @H@@@Q. ********  JW

)@@G@@(2) , + CALL(2,I) @^@@@Q          +         0   @#@@@Q          $END    KF

)@@G@@**** R$INF - CALLS 'RINF$' AND INVOKES 'ELT$'                  *******  KL
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ******** S$ELT - CALLS 'SELT$' WITH PARAMETER #                 KM
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ******** D$USE - CALLS 'DUSE$' WITH FILE$NAME(MAY BEKN
)@@G@@ R.J.)         *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************************KO
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@QP         $PROC     1    . A PKP
)@@G@@ARAMETER SPECIFIES # OF XQT PARAMETERS EXPECTED,@D@@@QR$INF**   $NAME   KQ
)@@G@@       .      OTHERWISE 3 ASSUMED   @F@@@Q          $LEVEL    0,1,0     KR
)@@G@@        . MAKE ELT$ LABELS GLOBAL   @E@@@Q          ELT$                KS
)@@G@@        . INVOKE 'ELT$' PROC  @F@@@Q          $LEVEL    0,0,0           KT
)@@G@@  . RETURN TO NORMAL LEVELING @B@@@QNN        $EQU      28*(3*(P=1)+P(1,KU
)@@G@@1))   @A@@@Q          L         A0,(NN,INF)     @ @@@Q          LMJ     KV
)@@G@@  X11,RINF$ @^@@@Q          J         ERR @^@@@Q          J         CONTKW
)@@G@@@^@@@QINF       RES       NN  @ @@@QERR       ER        PRINT$    @ @@@QKX
)@@G@@          ER        EXIT$     @]@@@QCONT      . @#@@@Q          $END    KY
)@@G@@@^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QS$ELT**   $NAME   @A@@@Q          $DKZ
)@@G@@O P(1)>0 , L,U A0,P(1,1)@^@@@Q          LMJ X11,SELT$ @#@@@Q          $ELA
)@@G@@ND    @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QD$USE**   $NAME   @C@@@Q      LB
)@@G@@    $DO P(1)>0 , DL A0,($CFS(P(1,1)DL))   @ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,LC
)@@G@@DUSE$ @#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. **********************LD
)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@@@Q. ******** SLE
)@@G@@OURCE OUTPUT PROCS - AIDS IN USING SSOR, SOR, AND ESOR   *******  @H@@@QLF
)@@G@@. ********                       SUBROUTINES                         ***LG
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********                                                  LH
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$SOR - SETS UP 'PARTBL', ASSIGNS FILLI
)@@G@@E AND CALLS 'SSOR'   *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,1) =   FILE $LJ
)@@G@@NAME(MAY BE R.J.)                *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,2LK
)@@G@@) = ELEMENT $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)               *******  @H@@@Q. ********  LL
)@@G@@       P(1,3) = VERSION $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)               *******  @H@@@QLM
)@@G@@. ********         P(0,1) = 1, IF NOT FIRST TIME CALLED              ***LN
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ******** S$OR  - CALLS 'SOR'                              LO
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,1) = (NWDS,ADDR)         LP
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,1),P(1,2) = ALQ
)@@G@@DDR,NWDS                         *******  @H@@@Q. ******** E$SOR - CALLSLR
)@@G@@ 'ESOR'                                      *******  @H@@@Q. **********LS
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @^@@@QLT
)@@G@@P         $PROC     1   @#@@@QS$SOR**   $NAME   @A@@@Q          $DO P(0,LU
)@@G@@1)=0 , GO CONT1   @B@@@Q          DL        A0,($CFS(P(1,1)DL))   @A@@@QLV
)@@G@@          DS        A0,PARTBL+27    @B@@@Q          DL        A0,($CFS(PLW
)@@G@@(1,2)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PARTBL+29    @C@@@Q          $DLX
)@@G@@O P(1)>2 , DL A0,($CFS(P(1,3)DL))   @B@@@Q          $DO P(1)>2 , DS A0,PLY
)@@G@@ARTBL+33    @#@@@QCONT1     $NAME   @A@@@Q          L         A0,(3,PARTLZ
)@@G@@BL+26)@^@@@Q          ER        CSF$@ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,SSOR$ MA
)@@G@@@^@@@Q          ER        ERR$@ @@@Q          $DO P(0,1) , $END   @^@@@QMB
)@@G@@          J         CONT@^@@@QPARTBL**  RES       26  @#@@@Q          '@MC
)@@G@@ASG'  @^@@@Q          $CFS(P(1,1)DL)@^@@@Q          $CFS(P(1,2)DL)@^@@@QMD
)@@G@@          RES       2   @^@@@Q          $CFS(P(1,3)DL)@^@@@Q          REME
)@@G@@S       8   @]@@@QCONT      . @#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QP         $PMF
)@@G@@ROC     1   @#@@@QS$OR**    $NAME   @A@@@Q          $DO P(1)=1 , L A0,P(MG
)@@G@@1,1)  @C@@@Q          $DO P(1)=2 , L A0,(P(1,2),P(1,1))     @ @@@Q      MH
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,SOR$  @^@@@Q          ER        ERR$@#@@@Q          $EMI
)@@G@@ND    @^@@@QE$SOR**   $PROC     0   @ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,ESOR$ MJ
)@@G@@@^@@@Q          ER        ERR$@#@@@Q          $END    @H@@@Q. **********MK
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @H@@@QML
)@@G@@. ******* TEST FACILITY FOR MASM ELEMENTS                            ***MM
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. *******                                                   MN
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ******* IF @MASM,T USED, FACILITY IS PROCED ONMO
)@@G@@ AND IF T2 OF        *******  @H@@@Q. ******* RUN CONDITION WORD IS = 2 MP
)@@G@@(@SETC 2), SNOOPY IS TURNED ON   *******  @H@@@Q. *******               MQ
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@Q. **********MR
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @#@@@QMS
)@@G@@TEST**    $PROC   @G@@@QMASMT*    $EQU      $PAR(0)**(1*/('Z'-'T')) . TEMT
)@@G@@ST MODE IF @MASM,T USED @C@@@RLCN       $EQU      $LCN              . SAMU
)@@G@@VE LC @ @@@Q          $IF       MASMT     @G@@@Q          J         CONTMV
)@@G@@1             . JUMP TO ANOTHER LOCATION COUNTER@B@@@R$(0)      '*TEST*'MW
)@@G@@  . FOR IDONLY$ USE     @]@R@Q$($LCN+2)   @]@@@R$(LCN+2)    @^@@@QSAVE  MX
)@@G@@    $RES      2   @D@@@QCONT1     DS        A0,SAVE           . SAVE A0,MY
)@@G@@A1    @E@@@Q          COND$                       . GET CONDITION WORD  MZ
)@@G@@@D@@@Q          AND       A0,(0770000)      . ISOLATE T2    @F@@@Q      NA
)@@G@@    TNE       A1,(020000)       . IF = 2, TURN ON SNOOPY    @^@@@Q      NB
)@@G@@    SLJ       TON$@D@@@Q          DL        A0,SAVE           . RESTORE NC
)@@G@@A0,A1 @H@@@Q          J         CONT2             . JUMP BACK TO ORIGINAND
)@@G@@L LOCATION COUNTER@#@R@Q$($LCN-2),CONT2   @#@T@R$(LCN-2),CONT2    @]@@@TNE
)@@G@@$(LCN),CONT2@#@@@R          $ELSE   @#@@@R$(0)      '      '@[@@@R$(LCN)NF
)@@G@@@#@@@Q          $ENDF   @#@@@Q          $END    @#@@@Q          $END    NG
)@@G@@_@@@@@(1,1)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PARTBL+27    @B@@@Q      NH
)@@G@@    DL        A0,($CFS(P(1,2)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PARTBL+NI
)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@#@@@@          $DEF    @ @@@@          $LEVEL    0,1,0     NJ
)@@G@@@^@@@@P         $PROC     *1  @ @@@@FORK$*    $NAME     'FORK$'   @ @@@@NK
)@@G@@TFORK$*   $NAME     'TFORK$'  @ @@@@          $DO       P(1)>0 , ;@H@@@@NL
)@@G@@          LA        12,+(OPT$$ +($GFORM 6,P(1,4),6,P(1,3),6,P(1,2),18,P(NM
)@@G@@1,1)))@ @@@@FORK$P*   $NAME     *'FORK$'  @ @@@@TFORK$P*  $NAME     *'TFNN
)@@G@@ORK$' @H@@@@          $DO       (P(0,0)='TFORK$')**(P(0)>1) , LA 13,+(EQNO
