)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ******* 1R2  -- SAVE R1 IN BRW
)@@G@@SEARCH                                 *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- RX
)@@G@@ADD SEARCH NOT EQUAL FACILITY TO BSEARCH           *******  @H@@@C. ****RY
)@@G@@***      -- OUTPUT BYTE # OF START OF FIELD IN GETFIELD        *******  RZ
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******      -- ALLOW ASCII BYTES IN ALL SUBROUTINES            SA
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- COMBINE BASE ADDRESS AND BYTE # IN OSB
)@@G@@NE INPUT       *******  @H@@@C. *******         REGISTER                SC
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- BYTE COMPARESD
)@@G@@ SUBROUTINE ADDED                      *******  @H@@@C. ******* 1R3  -- SE
)@@G@@FINDFIELD SUBROUTINE ADDED                         *******  @H@@@C. ****SF
)@@G@@***      -- BGET SUBROUTINE ADDED                              *******  SG
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******      -- BYTE COMPARE SUBROUTINE INPUTS CHANGED          SH
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- BSEARCH AND STUFF SUBROUTINES STREAMSI
)@@G@@LINED          *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- CONVERTED TO MASM FORMATSJ
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ******* 1R4  -- SAVE A1 IN FSK
)@@G@@INDFIELD                               *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- SL
)@@G@@DON'T SAVE A2 IN BMOVE                             *******  @H@@@C. ****SM
)@@G@@***      -- EXPAND SUBROUTINES TO PERFORM AUTO CONVERSION      *******  SN
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******      -- BYTE BLANK SUBROUTINE ADDED                     SO
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- CHANGE DEFINITION OF R1 FOR 'BSEARCHSP
)@@G@@' & 'GETFIELD' *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- STREAMLINE 'FINDFIELD'  SQ
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- CHANGE OUTPUSR
)@@G@@T OF 'FINDFIELD'                       *******  @H@@@C. ******* 1R5  -- SS
)@@G@@UPGRADE 'BINT' TO HANDLE OCTAL AND NEGATIVE        *******  @H@@@C. ****ST
)@@G@@***         INTEGERS                                           *******  SU
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******      -- UPGRADE 'GETFIELD' TO HANDLE SUBFIELDS AS WELL  SV
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         AS FIELDS (DELINEATED BY ','S)      SW
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- CHANGE 'BINT' TO HAVE ERSX
)@@G@@ROR EXIT                   *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- BYTE TDATE SSY
)@@G@@UBROUTINE ADDED                        *******  @H@@@C. *******      -- SZ
)@@G@@CHANGE OUTPUT OF 'GETFIELD'                        *******  @H@@@C. ****TA
)@@G@@*** 1R6  -- BYTE FILE-NAME SUBROUTINE ADDED                    *******  TB
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******      -- ALLOW 'BTDATE' TO HANDLE ASCII                  TC
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ******* 2R1  -- FIX BUG IN 'BFILE'                  TD
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* 2R2  -- GET SUBFIELD SUBROUTINE TE
)@@G@@ADDED                      *******  @H@@@D. ******* 2R3  -- ASCII BUG INTF
)@@G@@ GETFIELD & GETSFIELD FIXED            *******  @H@@@C. *******         TG
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****TH
)@@G@@**********************************************************************  TI
)@@G@@@#@@@C$(1)      AXR$    @H@C@B. ****************************************TJ
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@C@B. *******      BYTE MOVE SUBROTK
)@@G@@UTINE (FIELDATA)                       *******  @H@C@B. *******         TL
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@C@B. ****TM
)@@G@@***           INPUT:  X1 - INPUT BASE ADDRESS                  *******  TN
)@@G@@@H@C@B. *******                   X2 - OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS              TO
)@@G@@   *******  @H@C@B. *******                   A0 - # OF BYTES TO MOVE   TP
)@@G@@               *******  @H@C@B. *******                   A1 - BYTE # OFTQ
)@@G@@ INPUT (0-FIRST)           *******  @H@C@B. *******                   A2TR
)@@G@@ - BYTE # OF OUTPUT                    *******  @H@C@B. *******         TS
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@C@B. ****TT
)@@G@@**********************************************************************  TU
)@@G@@@^@C@BBMOVE*    +         0   @E@C@B          DS        A3,SAVE         TV
)@@G@@  . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @C@B          L         A4,A1     @^@C@B      TW
)@@G@@    SZ        A3  @G@C@B          DI,U      A3,6              . CALC WD TX
)@@G@@# AND BYTE # OF INPUT   @ @C@B          LSSL      A4,33     @^@C@B      TY
)@@G@@    LDSL      A3,3@ @C@B          LXI,U     A3,0600001@ @C@B          L TZ
)@@G@@        J0,A3     @ @C@B          L         A4,A2     @^@C@B          SZUA
)@@G@@        A3  @G@C@B          DI,U      A3,6              . CALC WD # AND UB
)@@G@@BYTE # OF OUTPUT  @ @C@B          LSSL      A4,33     @^@C@B          LDUC
)@@G@@SL      A3,3@ @C@B          LXI,U     A3,0600001@ @C@B          L       UD
)@@G@@  J1,A3     @ @C@B          L,U       SR1,0     @ @C@B          L,U     UE
)@@G@@  SR2,0     @ @C@B          L         A3,A0     @^@C@B          LSSL    UF
)@@G@@  A3,9@ @C@B          A         A3,A0     @ @C@B          LSSL      A3,1UG
)@@G@@8     @ @C@B          L         SR3,A3    @^@C@B          BM        0,X1UH
)@@G@@@F@C@B          DL        A3,SAVE           . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    UI
)@@G@@@C@C@B          J         *BMOVE            . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@CUJ
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************UK
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE MOVE SUBROUTINE                              UL
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       UM
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUTUN
)@@G@@ BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - (UO
)@@G@@BYTE #,OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS)                  *******  @H@@@C. *******   UP
)@@G@@      A0 - # OF BYTES TO MOVE                            *******  @H@@@CUQ
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***UR
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BMOVE                   US
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       UT
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. **********************************UU
)@@G@@****************************************  @[@@@CBMOVE*@E@@@C          DSUV
)@@G@@        A1,SBMOVE         . SAVE REGISTERS USED @A@@@C          S       UW
)@@G@@  X3,SBMOVE+2     @ @@@C          L,H1      A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L UX
)@@G@@        A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATEUY
)@@G@@ J0   @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @ @@@C          L,H2      A2,BUZ
)@@G@@ASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,X2     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFVA
)@@G@@F             . GENERATE J1   @ @@@C          L         J1,A1     @ @@@CVB
)@@G@@          L         J2,(1*/35)@ @@@C          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@CVC
)@@G@@          L,U       SR2,0     @ @@@C          L         A1,A0     @^@@@CVD
)@@G@@          LSSL      A1,9@ @@@C          A         A1,A0     @ @@@C      VE
)@@G@@    LSSL      A1,18     @ @@@C          L         SR3,A1    @E@@@C      VF
)@@G@@    L,H1      A1,BASCII         . GET INPUT ASCII KEY @H@@@C          L,VG
)@@G@@U       X3,*CONVT,A1      . GET CORRESPONDING TRANSLATE TABLE     @G@@@CVH
)@@G@@          XOR,H2    A1,BASCII         . COMPARE TO OUTPUT ASCII KEY     VI
)@@G@@@H@@@C          EX        BMOVET,A2         . DO 'BM' IF KEYS =, OTHERWIVJ
)@@G@@SE DO 'BMT' @F@@@C          DL        A1,SBMOVE         . RESTORE REGISTVK
)@@G@@ERS USED    @A@@@C          L         X3,SBMOVE+2     @C@@@C          J VL
)@@G@@        0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@B. ****************VM
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@C. ****VN
)@@G@@*** BYTE GET SUBROUTINE                                        *******  VO
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                                                         VP
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)    VQ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - BYTE               VR
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. *******                     VS
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING VT
)@@G@@SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BGET                             *******  @H@@@C. ****VU
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  VV
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ****************************************************************VW
)@@G@@**********  @[@@@CBGET* @E@@@C          DS        A1,SBGET          . SAVX
)@@G@@VE REGISTER USED  @F@@@C          SPD       A0                . TURN ON VY
)@@G@@CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@C          OR,U      A0,1@^@@@C          LPD     VZ
)@@G@@  0,A1@ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,XWA
)@@G@@1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @@@CWB
)@@G@@          S         A1,J0     @C@@@C          L,4       A0,0,*X1        WC
)@@G@@  . GET BYTE@F@@@C          SPD       A1                . TURN OFF CHARAWD
)@@G@@CTER MODE   @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1WE
)@@G@@@F@@@C          DL        A1,SBGET          . RESTORE REGISTER USED     WF
)@@G@@@ @@@C          J         0,X11     @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************WG
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@C@B. ****WH
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  WI
)@@G@@@H@C@B. *******     BYTE TO INTEGER SUBROUTINE (FIELDATA)               WJ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE TO INTEGER SUBROUTINE                  WK
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@B. *******                                 WL
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #WM
)@@G@@,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@C@B. *******     INPUWN
)@@G@@T:  X1 - INPUT BASE ADDRESS                        *******  @H@C@B. ****WO
)@@G@@***             A1 - BYTE # OF INPUT STRING                    *******  WP
)@@G@@@H@C@B. *******             A0 - # OF INPUT BYTES                       WQ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         A0 - # OF INPUT BYTES               WR
)@@G@@               *******  @^@C@B. *******     OUTPUT: A2@H@@@C. ******* OUWS
)@@G@@TPUT: A2                                                 *******  @H@@@CWT
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***WU
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BINT                    WV
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                   J ILLEGAL-INTEGER   WW
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                   J NORMALWX
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@B. *******               WY
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@B. **********WZ
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @^@C@BXA
)@@G@@BINT*     +         0   @[@@@CBINT* @E@C@B          S         A3,SAVE   XB
)@@G@@        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @E@@@C          DS        A0,SBINT        XC
)@@G@@   . SAVE REGISTERS USED@ @@@C          S         X1,SBINT+2@A@@@C      XD
)@@G@@    S         X10,SBINT+3     @G@@@C          L,U       X10,1,X11       XE
)@@G@@  . SETUP X10 FOR NORMAL RETURN     @E@@@C          SZ        NEGKEY    XF
)@@G@@        . CLEAR NEGATIVE KEY  @ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @D@@@CXG
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,BGET          . GET NEXT CHAR @D@@@C          TEXH
)@@G@@        A0,NEG,A2         . IS IT '-'?    @B@@@C          J         $+4 XI
)@@G@@              . NO@F@@@C          SP1       NEGKEY            . YES, SETXJ
)@@G@@ NEGATIVE KEY     @D@@@C          A         X1,(1,0)          . BUMP CHAXK
)@@G@@R PTR @D@@@C          LMJ       X11,BGET          . GET NEXT CHAR @D@@@CXL
)@@G@@          TNE       A0,ZERO,A2        . IS IT '0'?    @G@@@C          J XM
)@@G@@        BINTC1            . YES, GO TO OCTAL INTEGER LOGIC  @E@@@C      XN
)@@G@@    L         A0,SBINT          . NO, RESTORE INPUT A0@E@@@C          TZXO
)@@G@@        NEGKEY            . IS NEGATIVE KEY SET?@H@@@C          AN,U    XP
)@@G@@  A0,1              . YES, REDUCE # OF CHARS INPUT BY 1     @G@@@C      XQ
)@@G@@    J         BINTC3            . GO TO DECIMAL INTEGER LOGIC     @G@@@CXR
)@@G@@BINTC1                                . OCTAL INTEGER LOGIC FOLLOWS     XS
)@@G@@@E@@@C          DS        A3,SBINT+4        . SAVE MORE REGISTERS @ @@@CXT
)@@G@@          S         A5,SBINT+6@G@@@C          L         A3,ZERO,A2      XU
)@@G@@  . SET UP LIMITS TO TEST CHARS     @G@@@C          AN,U      A3,1      XV
)@@G@@        . CHARS MUST BE BETWEEN 0 AND 7   @A@@@C          L         A4,SXW
)@@G@@EVEN,A2     @F@@@C          SZ        A5                . BUILD BINARY VXX
)@@G@@ALUE IN A5  @F@@@C          L         A1,SBINT          . INITIALIZE LOOXY
)@@G@@P COUNTER   @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@ @@@C          TZ        NEGKXZ
)@@G@@EY    @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@E@@@CBINTL     LMJ       X11,BGET  YA
)@@G@@        . GET CHARS 1 BY 1    @G@@@C          TW        A3,A0           YB
)@@G@@  . IS CHAR BETWEEN '0' AND '7'?    @G@@@C          J         BINTC1A   YC
)@@G@@        . NO, NOT LEGAL OCTAL INTEGER     @G@@@C          AN        A0,ZYD
)@@G@@ERO,A2        . CONVERT CHARACTER TO BINARY     @G@@@C          MSI,U   YE
)@@G@@  A5,8              . MULTIPLY PREVIOUS RESULT BY 8   @D@@@C          A YF
)@@G@@        A5,A0             . ADD NEW VALUE @D@@@C          A         X1,(YG
)@@G@@1,0)          . BUMP CHAR PTR @F@@@C          JGD       A1,BINTL        YH
)@@G@@  . IS SCAN OF FIELD COMPLETE?@H@@@C          L         A2,A5           YI
)@@G@@  . YES, A5 HAS CONVERTED OCTAL INTEGER   @ @@@C          J         BINTYJ
)@@G@@C2    @G@@@CBINTC1A   AN,U      X10,1             . BAD FORMAT, SETUP FOYK
)@@G@@R BAD RETURN@F@@@CBINTC2    DL        A3,SBINT+4        . RESTORE REGISTYL
)@@G@@ERS USED    @ @@@C          L         A5,SBINT+6@F@@@C          J       YM
)@@G@@  BINTE             . GO TO NORMAL EXIT LOGIC   @ @C@B          L       YN
)@@G@@  A3,A1     @F@@@CBINTC3    L         A1,X1             . DECIMAL INTEGEYO
)@@G@@R LOGIC     @^@C@B          SZ        A2  @G@C@B          DI,U      A2,6YP
)@@G@@              . CALC WORD # AND BYTE # OF INPUT @ @C@B          LSSL    YQ
)@@G@@  A3,33     @^@C@B          LDSL      A2,3@ @C@B          LXI,U     A2,0YR
)@@G@@600001@D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @C@BYS
)@@G@@          L         J0,A2     @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @ @@@BYT
)@@G@@          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@B          L,U       SR2,0     @ @@@BYU
)@@G@@          L         A2,A0     @ @@@B          LSSL      A2,27     @ @@@BYV
)@@G@@          L         SR3,A2    @ @C@B          BI        A2,0,X1   @ @@@CYW
)@@G@@          BI        A2,0,*X1  @G@C@B          TZ,H2     SR3             YX
)@@G@@  . IF ANY ERROR OCCURRED, A2=0     @F@@@C          TZ,H2     SR3       YY
)@@G@@        . IF ANY ERROR OCCURRED,    @^@C@B          L,U       A2,0@E@@@CYZ
)@@G@@          AN,U      X10,1             .   TAKE BAD RETURN   @F@C@B      ZA
)@@G@@    L         A3,SAVE           . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @E@@@CBINTE ZB
)@@G@@    L         A1,A2             . IF NEGATIVE KEY SET,@E@@@C          TZZC
)@@G@@        NEGKEY            .  SET COMPLEMENT A2  @ @@@C          SN      ZD
)@@G@@  A1,A2     @F@@@C          DL        A0,SBINT          . RESTORE REGISTZE
)@@G@@ERS USED    @ @@@C          L         X1,SBINT+2@ @@@C          L       ZF
)@@G@@  X11,X10   @A@@@C          L         X10,SBINT+3     @C@C@B          J ZG
)@@G@@        *BINT             . RETURN  @C@@@C          J         0,X11     ZH
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************ZI
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE BLANK SUBZJ
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                      *******  @H@@@C. *******   ZK
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CZL
)@@G@@. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   ***ZM
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         A0 - # OF BLANKS TO STORE                 ZN
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       ZO
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,ZP
)@@G@@BBLANK                           *******  @H@@@C. *******               ZQ
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. **********ZR
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @]@@@CZS
)@@G@@BBLANK*     @E@@@C          DS        A0,SAVE           . SAVE REGISTERSZT
)@@G@@ USED @ @@@C          S         A2,SAVE+2 @F@@@C          SPD       A1  ZU
)@@G@@              . TURN ON CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@C          OR,U      A1,1ZV
)@@G@@@^@@@C          LPD       0,A2@ @@@C          L         A2,BASCII @ @@@CZW
)@@G@@          L         A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLJ       STUFF           ZX
)@@G@@  . GENERATE J0   @ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @^@@@C          ANZY
)@@G@@,U      A0,1@A@@@C          L         A1,BLANKS,A2    @D@@@C          S,ZZ
)@@G@@4       A1,0,*X1          . STORE BLANKS  @ @@@C          JGD       A0,$AA
)@@G@@-1    @F@@@C          SPD       A1                . TURN OFF CHARACTER MAB
)@@G@@ODE   @^@@@C          AN,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1@F@@@CAC
)@@G@@          DL        A0,SAVE           . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    @ @@@CAD
)@@G@@          L         A2,SAVE+2 @ @@@C          J         0,X11     @[@@@CAE
)@@G@@.     @H@@@C. **********************************************************AF
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE SEARCH SUBROUTINE                AG
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           AH
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (AI
)@@G@@BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******   AJ
)@@G@@      A0 - SEARCH BYTE (IF=-BYTE SEARCH NOT EQUAL USED)  *******  @H@@@CAK
)@@G@@. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    ***AL
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A2 - BYTE # OF FOUND BYTE                 AM
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       AN
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,AO
)@@G@@BSEARCH                          *******  @H@@@C. *******               AP
)@@G@@      J NOFIND                               *******  @H@@@C. *******   AQ
)@@G@@                  J FIND                                 *******  @H@@@CAR
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***AS
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. **********************************************************AT
)@@G@@****************  @]@@@CBSEARCH*    @E@@@C          DS        A0,SAVE   AU
)@@G@@        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         R1,SAVE+2 @F@@@CAV
)@@G@@          SPD       A1                . TURN ON CHARACTER MODE    @^@@@CAW
)@@G@@          OR,U      A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A2@ @@@C          L AX
)@@G@@        A2,BASCII @ @@@C          L         A1,X1     @D@@@C          SLAY
)@@G@@J       STUFF             . GENERATE J0   @ @@@C          L         J0,AAZ
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          L         A1,X1             . CALC # OF BYTES TO SBA
)@@G@@EARCH @ @@@C          SSL       A1,18     @ @@@C          AN        A1,RBB
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          JP        A1,BSNO           . SKIP SEARCH IF COUNTBC
)@@G@@ <=0  @ @@@C          SN        A1,R1     @E@@@C          TN        A0  BD
)@@G@@              . IF A0<0, USE SNE    @E@@@C          J         BSC1      BE
)@@G@@        .   OTHERWISE USE SE  @ @@@C          LN        A1,A0     @ @@@CBF
)@@G@@          SNE,4     A1,0,*X1  @^@@@C          J         BSNO@^@@@C      BG
)@@G@@    J         BSC2@E@@@CBSC1      SE,4      A0,0,*X1          . SEARCH FBH
)@@G@@OR BYTE     @C@@@C          J         BSNO              . NO FIND @F@@@CBI
)@@G@@BSC2      L         A1,J0             . CALC BYTE # OF FOUND BYTE @^@@@CBJ
)@@G@@          LXI,U     A1,0@^@@@C          DSL       A1,3@ @@@C          L BK
)@@G@@        A0,BASCII @ @@@C          MSI       A1,NBIT,A0@A@@@C          SSBL
)@@G@@L       A2,*NSHIFT,A0   @ @@@C          A         A2,A1     @^@@@C      BM
)@@G@@    AN,U      A2,1@ @@@C          A,U       X11,1     @E@@@CBSNO      SPBN
)@@G@@D       A1                . CLEAR CHARACTER MODE@^@@@C          AN,U    BO
)@@G@@  A1,1@^@@@C          LPD       0,A1@ @@@C          DL        A0,SAVE   BP
)@@G@@@ @@@C          L         R1,SAVE+2 @C@@@C          J         0,X11     BQ
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************BR
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@C. ******* BYTE COMPARE SBS
)@@G@@UBROUTINE                                    *******  @H@@@C. *******   BT
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CBU
)@@G@@. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS 1)                 ***BV
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS 2)        BW
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         A0 - # OF BYTES TO COMPARE    BX
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - 0 IF 2 STRINGBY
)@@G@@S COMPARE                        *******  @H@@@C. *******               BZ
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* CACA
)@@G@@LLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BCOMP                            *******  @H@@@CCB
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***CC
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. **********************************************************CD
)@@G@@****************  @[@@@CBCOMP*@E@@@C          DS        A1,SBCOMP       CE
)@@G@@  . SAVE REGISTERS USED @A@@@C          S         X2,SBCOMP+2     @A@@@CCF
)@@G@@          S         X1,SBCOMP+3     @A@@@C          S         X11,SBCOMPCG
)@@G@@+4    @ @@@C          L,H1      A2,BASCII @F@@@C          TNE,H2    A2,BCH
)@@G@@ASCII         . IS CONVERSION IMPLIED?    @B@@@C          J         BCOMCI
)@@G@@PC            . NO@G@@@C          L,U       X2,BUFF           . CONVERT CJ
)@@G@@1ST STRING INTO BUFF    @ @@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @F@@@C      CK
)@@G@@    L         X11,SBCOMP+4      . RESTORE RETURN ADDRESS    @F@@@C      CL
)@@G@@    L         X1,X2             . USE BUFF FOR COMPARISON   @A@@@C      CM
)@@G@@    L         X2,SBCOMP+2     @ @@@C          L,H2      A2,BASCII @ @@@CCN
)@@G@@BCOMPC    L         A1,X1     @C@@@C          SLJ       STUFF           CO
)@@G@@  . SETUP J0@ @@@C          L         J0,A1     @ @@@C          L       CP
)@@G@@  A1,X2     @C@@@C          SLJ       STUFF             . SETUP J1@ @@@CCQ
)@@G@@          L         J1,A1     @ @@@C          L,U       SR1,0     @ @@@CCR
)@@G@@          L,U       SR2,0     @ @@@C          S         A0,A1     @^@@@CCS
)@@G@@          LSSL      A0,9@ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @ @@@C      CT
)@@G@@    LSSL      A0,18     @D@@@C          L         SR3,A0            . SECU
)@@G@@TUP SR3     @D@@@C          BC        A0,,*X1           . BYTE COMPARE  CV
)@@G@@@F@@@C          DL        A1,SBCOMP         . RESTORE REGISTERS USED    CW
)@@G@@@A@@@C          L         X1,SBCOMP+3     @C@@@C          J         0,X1CX
)@@G@@1             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************************CY
)@@G@@**********************************************  @C@@@C. ******* GET NEXTCZ
)@@G@@ FIELD SUBROUTINE   *******   @H@@@C. ******* (FIELDS ARE DELINEATED BY DA
)@@G@@SPACES)                          *******  @H@@@C. *******               DB
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* INDC
)@@G@@PUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@CDD
)@@G@@. *******         X2 - (BYTE #,OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS)                  ***DE
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING           DF
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         R2 - MAX # OF BYTES TO MOVE   DG
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - # OF BYTES INDH
)@@G@@ FIELD                           *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - BDI
)@@G@@YTE # OF START OF FIELD                      *******  @H@@@C. *******   DJ
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CDK
)@@G@@. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,GETFIELD                         ***DL
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND                      DM
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FIND            DN
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           DO
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. **********************DP
)@@G@@****************************************************  @]@@@CGETFIELD*   DQ
)@@G@@@E@@@C          SZ        SFIELDKEY         . CLEAR SUBFIELD KEY  @E@@@CDR
)@@G@@          J         GETSFIELD+1       . USE GETSFIELD LOGIC @[@@@C.     DS
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ****************************************************************DT
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@C. ******* GET NEXT SUBFIELD SUBROUTINE                DU
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* (SUBFIELDS ARE DELINEATED BY SPADV
)@@G@@CES OR COMMAS)             *******  @H@@@C. *******                     DW
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  DX
)@@G@@X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. ****DY
)@@G@@***         X2 - (BYTE #,OUTPUT BASE ADDRESS)                  *******  DZ
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                 EA
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         R2 - MAX # OF BYTES TO MOVE         EB
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - # OF BYTES IN FIELDEC
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - BYTE # ED
)@@G@@OF START OF FIELD                      *******  @H@@@C. *******         EE
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****EF
)@@G@@*** CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,GETSFIELD                        *******  EG
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND                            EH
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FIND                  EI
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******                                 EJ
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ****************************EK
)@@G@@**********************************************  @]@@@CGETSFIELD*  @E@@@CEL
)@@G@@          SP1       SFIELDKEY         . SET SUBFIELD KEY    @E@@@C      EM
)@@G@@    S         X11,SAVE+5        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S EN
)@@G@@        A2,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          S         X1,SAVE+4 @ @@@C          S EO
)@@G@@        X3,SAVE+6 @G@@@D          L         A0,BASCII         . REVERSE EP
)@@G@@ASCII KEYS IN BASCII    @ @@@D          SSC       A0,18     @ @@@D      EQ
)@@G@@    S         A0,BASCII @E@@@D          S         A0,X3             . SAER
)@@G@@VE IN X3 ALSO     @D@D@C          L,H1      X3,BASCII         . ASCII KEES
)@@G@@Y     @A@@@C          LN        A0,SPACE,X3     @F@@@C          LMJ     ET
)@@G@@  X11,BSEARCH       . SEARCH FOR START OF FIELD @C@@@C          J       EU
)@@G@@  GETFE             . NO-FIND @G@@@C          S         A2,TEMP         EV
)@@G@@  . SAVE BYTE # OF START OF FIELD   @E@@@C          LXI       X1,A2     EW
)@@G@@        . FIND NEXT BLANK     @A@@@C          L         A0,SPACE,X3     EX
)@@G@@@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     @F@@@C          L         A2,REY
)@@G@@1             . NO-FIND, SET TO LAST CHAR @F@@@C          L         A1,AEZ
)@@G@@2             . SAVE BYTE # OF NEXT BLANK @E@@@C          L         A0,CFA
)@@G@@OMMA,X3       . FIND NEXT COMMA     @H@@@C          TZ        SFIELDKEY FB
)@@G@@        . IF SUBFIELD KEY SET, SKIP COMMA SEARCH@A@@@C          LMJ     FC
)@@G@@  X11,BSEARCH     @F@@@C          L         A2,R1             . NO-FIND,FD
)@@G@@ SET TO LAST CHAR @F@@@C          TG        A2,A1             . SET A2 TFE
)@@G@@O MIN CHAR POS    @ @@@C          L         A2,A1     @E@@@C          L FF
)@@G@@        A0,A2             . BYTE # OF ' ' OR ','@F@@@C          AN      FG
)@@G@@  A0,TEMP           . CALC # OF BYTES TO MOVE   @E@@@C          TG      FH
)@@G@@  A0,R2             . CHECK FOR MAX SIZE  @ @@@C          L         A0,RFI
)@@G@@2     @E@@@D          L         A1,BASCII         . RESTORE ASCII KEYS  FJ
)@@G@@@ @@@D          SSC       A1,18     @ @@@D          S         A1,BASCII FK
)@@G@@@E@@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE FIELD TO OUTPUT@D@@@CFL
)@@G@@          L         X11,SAVE+5        . RESTORE X11   @F@@@C          A,FM
)@@G@@U       X11,1             . POINT TO NORMAL RETURN    @ @@@C          L FN
)@@G@@        A1,TEMP   @ @@@C          AN        A2,A1     @ @@@C          L FO
)@@G@@        A0,A2     @D@@@C          J         $+2               . NORMAL RFP
)@@G@@ETURN @D@@@CGETFE     L         X11,SAVE+5        . RESTORE X11   @ @@@CFQ
)@@G@@          L         A2,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          L         X1,SAVE+4 @ @@@CFR
)@@G@@          L         X3,SAVE+6 @C@@@C          J         0,X11           FS
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. ****************************************FT
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@C. ******* FIND GIVEN FIELD SUBFU
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                *******  @H@@@C. *******         FV
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****FW
)@@G@@*** INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,BASE ADDRESS OF BLOCK)                *******  FX
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******         X2 - (BYTE #,BASE ADDRESS OF FIELD)             FY
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN BLOCK       FZ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******         A2 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN GA
)@@G@@FIELD                      *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - BYTE # GB
)@@G@@IN BLOCK WHERE FIELD FOUND             *******  @H@@@C. *******         GC
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****GD
)@@G@@*** CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,FINDFIELD                        *******  GE
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND                            GF
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FIND                  GG
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******                                 GH
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ****************************GI
)@@G@@**********************************************  @]@@@CFINDFIELD*  @E@@@CGJ
)@@G@@          S         X11,SAVE+2        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C      GK
)@@G@@    DS        A1,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          S         X1,SAVE+5 @H@@@C      GL
)@@G@@    AN        A1,A2             . CALC # OF TIMES TO COMPARE FIELDS     GM
)@@G@@@ @@@C          S         A1,R1     @ @@@C          L         A0,A2     GN
)@@G@@@E@@@C          LMJ       X11,BCOMP         . COMPARE 2 FIELDS    @D@@@CGO
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,FINDF          . FIELD FOUND   @E@@@C          A GP
)@@G@@        X1,(1,0)          . BUMP BYTE # OF BLOCK@F@@@C          JGD     GQ
)@@G@@  R1,$-4            . CHECK FOR END OF BLOCK    @G@@@C          J       GR
)@@G@@  FINDN             . END OF BLOCK, FIELD NOT FOUND   @G@@@CFINDF     L GS
)@@G@@        A0,X1             . GET BYTE # WHERE FIELD FOUND    @ @@@C      GT
)@@G@@    SSL       A0,18     @D@@@C          L         X11,SAVE+2        . REGU
)@@G@@STORE X11   @F@@@C          A,U       X11,1             . POINT TO NORMAGV
)@@G@@L RETURN    @D@@@C          J         $+2               . NORMAL RETURN GW
)@@G@@@D@@@CFINDN     L         X11,SAVE+2        . RESTORE X11   @ @@@C      GX
)@@G@@    DL        A1,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          L         X1,SAVE+5 @C@@@C      GY
)@@G@@    J         0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********GZ
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @H@@@CHA
)@@G@@. ******* CONVERT TIME/DATE STRING TO TDATE$ FORMAT SUBROUTINE       ***HB
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* (STRINGS CAN BE OF FORM: 'HH:MM:SS' OR 'MM/DD/YY')HC
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       HD
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUTHE
)@@G@@ BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - #HF
)@@G@@ OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUHG
)@@G@@TPUT: A0 - TDATE$ WORD                                   *******  @H@@@CHH
)@@G@@. *******         A1 - BYTE # AFTER FIELD                            ***HI
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                                                   HJ
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BTDATE      HK
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J ERROHL
)@@G@@R                                *******  @H@@@C. *******               HM
)@@G@@      J NORMAL                               *******  @H@@@C. *******   HN
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CHO
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************HP
)@@G@@****  @]@@@CBTDATE*     @E@@@C          S         X11,10            . SAHQ
)@@G@@VE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         X1,SBTDATE@A@@@C          DSHR
)@@G@@        A1,SBTDATE+1    @A@@@C          S         X2,SBTDATE+3    @A@@@CHS
)@@G@@          S         A3,SBTDATE+4    @D@@@C          L         A0,BASCII HT
)@@G@@        . ASCII KEY     @G@@@C          LSSL      A0,18             . SHHU
)@@G@@IFT H1 TO H2 FOR GETFIELD     @ @@@C          S         A0,BASCII @D@@@CHV
)@@G@@          SZ        TDATEA            . CLEAR OUTPUT  @E@@@C          L,HW
)@@G@@U       X2,BUFF           . EXTRACT NEXT FIELD  @^@@@C          L,U     HX
)@@G@@  R2,8@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,GETFIELD    @D@@@C          J       HY
)@@G@@  BTDATEE+1         . NO MORE FIELDS@F@@@C          A         A0,A1     HZ
)@@G@@        . CALC BYTE # AFTER FIELD   @C@@@C          S         A0,SBTDATEIA
)@@G@@+1      . SAVE    @F@@@C          L,U       A0,'/'            . IS FIELDIB
)@@G@@ DATE OR TIME?    @ @@@C          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @C@@@C          J IC
)@@G@@        TDATET            . TIME    @D@@@C          TE,S6     A0,BUFF   ID
)@@G@@        . CHECK FORMAT  @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . FOIE
)@@G@@RMAT ERROR  @^@@@C          L,U       A2,0@ @@@C          L,U       A3,1IF
)@@G@@2     @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@CIG
)@@G@@          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@CIH
)@@G@@          L,S2      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@CII
)@@G@@          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0           IJ
)@@G@@  . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1       IK
)@@G@@  . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOIL
)@@G@@R OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,U       A3,31     @D@@@C          L,S4    IM
)@@G@@  A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'DD'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    IN
)@@G@@@ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S5      A1,BUFF   IO
)@@G@@@ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     IP
)@@G@@@F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    IQ
)@@G@@@D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C      IR
)@@G@@    S,S2      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,IS
)@@G@@U       A2,64     @ @@@C          L,U       A3,99     @D@@@C          L,IT
)@@G@@S1      A0,BUFF+1         . CONVERT 'YY'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'IU
)@@G@@0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BIV
)@@G@@UFF+1 @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,AIW
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMIIX
)@@G@@TS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @D@@@CIY
)@@G@@          AN,U      A0,64             . MODULO 64     @E@@@C          S,IZ
)@@G@@S3      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L       JA
)@@G@@  A0,TDATEA         . GET OUTPUT    @C@@@C          J         BTDATEE   JB
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @F@@@CTDATET    L,U       A0,':'            . CHECK FOJC
)@@G@@R FORMAT ERROR    @ @@@C          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @D@@@C          J JD
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @ @@@C          TE,S6     A0,BJE
)@@G@@UFF   @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @^@@@CJF
)@@G@@          LN,U      A2,1@ @@@C          L,U       A3,23     @D@@@C      JG
)@@G@@    L,S1      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'HH'  @ @@@C          AN,U    JH
)@@G@@  A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2    JI
)@@G@@  A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A       JJ
)@@G@@  A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIJK
)@@G@@N LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     JL
)@@G@@@E@@@C          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@CJM
)@@G@@          L,U       A3,59     @D@@@C          L,S4      A0,BUFF         JN
)@@G@@  . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSJO
)@@G@@I,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S5      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          ANJP
)@@G@@,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TWJQ
)@@G@@        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J JR
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S2      A0,TJS
)@@G@@DATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF+1 JT
)@@G@@        . CONVERT 'SS'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C      JU
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BUFF+1 @ @@@C      JV
)@@G@@    AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C      JW
)@@G@@    TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C      JX
)@@G@@    J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @ @@@C          S,S3    JY
)@@G@@  A0,TDATEA @H@@@C          L,S1      A0,TDATEA         . CONVERT HH,MM,JZ
)@@G@@SS TO SECS PAST MIDNIGHT@ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,60     @ @@@C      KA
)@@G@@    A,S2      A0,TDATEA @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,60     @ @@@C      KB
)@@G@@    A,S3      A0,TDATEA @F@@@CBTDATEE   A,U       X10,1             . POKC
)@@G@@INT TO NORMAL RETURN    @G@@@C          L         A1,BASCII         . REKD
)@@G@@STORE BASCII TO ORIGINAL VALUE@ @@@C          SSL       A1,18     @ @@@CKE
)@@G@@          S         A1,BASCII @ @@@C          L         X1,SBTDATE@A@@@CKF
)@@G@@          DL        A1,SBTDATE+1    @A@@@C          L         X2,SBTDATEKG
)@@G@@+3    @A@@@C          L         A3,SBTDATE+4    @C@@@C          J       KH
)@@G@@  0,X10             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************KI
)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@@@C. ******* EXKJ
)@@G@@TRACT FILE NAME STRING SUBROUTINE                        *******  @H@@@CKK
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***KL
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUT BASE ADDRESS)          KM
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - # OF BYTES IN INPUT STRINKN
)@@G@@G                    *******  @H@@@C. *******         X2 - OUTPUT BUFFERKO
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: OUT,+1KP
)@@G@@  - QUALIFIER                                *******  @H@@@C. *******   KQ
)@@G@@      OUT+2,3 - FILE-NAME                                *******  @H@@@CKR
)@@G@@. *******         OUT+4   - CYCLE (OCTAL)                            ***KS
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******         A0 = # OF BYTES IN FIELD                  KT
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 = BYTE # OF START OF FIELD KU
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                           KV
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENKW
)@@G@@CE: LMJ X11,BFILE                            *******  @H@@@C. *******   KX
)@@G@@                  J ERROR                                *******  @H@@@CKY
)@@G@@. *******                     J NORMAL                               ***KZ
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                                                   LA
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. **********************************************LB
)@@G@@****************************  @[@@@CBFILE*@E@@@C          S         X11,LC
)@@G@@X10           . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         X1,SBFILE LD
)@@G@@@A@@@C          S         X2,SBFILE+1     @A@@@C          S         X3,SLE
)@@G@@BFILE+2     @A@@@C          DS        A2,SBFILE+6     @E@@@C          L,LF
)@@G@@U       X2,BUFF           . FIND LIMITS OF FIELD@ @@@C          L,U     LG
)@@G@@  R2,46     @A@@@C          LMJ       X11,GETFIELD    @F@@@C          J LH
)@@G@@        BFILEE+1          . NO FIELD FOUND, ERROR     @F@@@C          DSLI
)@@G@@        A0,SBFILE+4       . SAVE GETFIELD OUTPUTS     @E@@@C          A LJ
)@@G@@        A0,A1             . CALC END BYTE #     @C@@@C          S       LK
)@@G@@  A0,SBFILE+3       . SAVE    @ @@@C          LXI       X1,A1     @F@@@CLL
)@@G@@          L         A3,A1             . A3 = CURRENT BYTE POINTER @D@@@CLM
)@@G@@          L         X2,SBFILE+1       . RESTORE X2    @D@@@C          L,LN
)@@G@@H1      X3,BASCII         . ASCII KEY     @E@@@C          L         A0,BLO
)@@G@@LANKS,X3      . INITIALIZE OUTPUT   @ @@@C          L         A1,A0     LP
)@@G@@@ @@@C          DS        A0,0,X2   @ @@@C          DS        A0,2,X2   LQ
)@@G@@@^@@@C          SZ        4,X2@D@@@C          L         A0,ASTER,X3     LR
)@@G@@  . SEARCH FOR '*'@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     @D@@@C      LS
)@@G@@    SZ        A2                . NONE FOUND    @E@@@C          S       LT
)@@G@@  A2,QUALKEY        . SAVE BYTE # OF '*'  @D@@@C          L         A0,LLU
)@@G@@PAREN,X3      . SEARCH FOR '('@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,BSEARCH     LV
)@@G@@@D@@@C          SZ        A2                . NONE FOUND    @E@@@C      LW
)@@G@@    S         A2,CYCLEKEY       . SAVE BYTE # OF '('  @F@@@C          L LX
)@@G@@        A0,QUALKEY        . IS THERE A QUALIFIER?     @B@@@C          JZLY
)@@G@@        A0,BFILEC         . NO@G@@@C          AN        A0,A3           LZ
)@@G@@  . CALC SIZE OF QUALIFIER SUBFIELD @F@@@C          LXI,U     X2,0      MA
)@@G@@        . MOVE QUALIFIER TO OUTPUT  @ @@@C          LMJ       X11,BMOVE MB
)@@G@@@E@@@C          L         A3,QUALKEY        . BUMP A3 PAST '*'    @^@@@CMC
)@@G@@          A,U       A3,1@ @@@C          LXI       X1,A3     @E@@@CBFILECMD
)@@G@@    L         A0,CYCLEKEY       . IS THERE A CYCLE?   @^@@@C          TNME
)@@G@@Z       A0  @E@@@C          L         A0,SBFILE+3       . NO, USE END BYMF
)@@G@@TE #  @H@@@C          AN        A0,A3             .   TO CALCULATE SIZE MG
)@@G@@OF FILE FIELD     @ @@@C          LXI,U     X2,12     @F@@@C          LMMH
)@@G@@J       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE FILE-NAME TO OUTPUT  @F@@@C          A,MI
)@@G@@U       A3,1,A0           . BUMP A3 PAST FILE-NAME    @E@@@C          TNMJ
)@@G@@Z       CYCLEKEY          . IS THERE A CYCLE?   @D@@@C          J       MK
)@@G@@  BFILEE            . NO, FINISHED  @F@@@C          LXI       X1,A3     ML
)@@G@@        . PREPARE TO EXTRACT CYCLE  @A@@@C          AN        A3,SBFILE+MM
)@@G@@3     @ @@@C          LN,XU     A0,1,A3   @F@@@C          LMJ       X11,MN
)@@G@@BINT          . CONVERT CYCLE TO BINARY   @D@@@C          J         BFILMO
)@@G@@EE+1          . FORMAT ERROR  @F@@@C          S         A2,4,X2         MP
)@@G@@  . STORE CYCLE IN OUTPUT     @G@@@CBFILEE    A,U       X10,1           MQ
)@@G@@  . GENERATE NORMAL RETURN ADDRESS  @ @@@C          L         X1,SBFILE MR
)@@G@@@A@@@C          L         X2,SBFILE+1     @A@@@C          L         X3,SMS
)@@G@@BFILE+2     @A@@@C          DL        A0,SBFILE+4     @A@@@C          DLMT
)@@G@@        A2,SBFILE+6     @C@@@C          J         0,X10             . REMU
)@@G@@TURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********************************************MV
)@@G@@****************************  @H@@@C. ******* J-REG STUFF LOCAL SUBROUTIMW
)@@G@@NE                               *******  @H@@@C. *******               MX
)@@G@@                                             *******  @H@@@C. ******* INMY
)@@G@@PUT: A1 = (BYTE #,X)                                     *******  @H@@@CMZ
)@@G@@. *******        A2 = ASCII KEY                                      ***NA
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A1 = CORRESPONDING J-REG                  NB
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       NC
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. **********************************ND
)@@G@@****************************************  @^@@@CSTUFF     +         0   NE
)@@G@@@D@@@C          DS        A2,STUFFD         . SAVE A2,A3    @ @@@C      NF
)@@G@@    L         A3,A2     @ @@@C          DSL       A1,54     @ @@@C      NG
)@@G@@    JZ        A2,STUFFC @ @@@C          DI        A1,NBIT,A3@A@@@C      NH

)@@G@@  A2,STUFFD         . RESTORE A2,A3 @ @@@C          J         *STUFF    NK
)@@G@@@H@@@C. ****************************************************************NL
)@@G@@**********  @^@C@BSAVE      RES       2   @[@@@C$(0)  @H@@@CBASCII*   + NM
)@@G@@        0                 . ASCII KEY (INITIALLY OFF FOR FIELDATA)@^@@@CNN

)@@G@@(2R2)                      *******  @H@@@!. ******* UPDATED BY LOU INFELAC
)@@G@@D, 03/14/79 (3R1)                      *******  @H@@@!. *******         AD
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@0@!. ****AE
)@@G@@*** THIS PROGRAM WILL PRINT PORTIONS OF SDF PRINT FILE.        *******  AF
)@@G@@@H@@@0. ******* THIS PROGRAM WILL PRINT PORTIONS OF AN SDF PRINT FILE.  AG
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. ******* TO DETERMINE WHICH PORTIONS OF A FILE TO PRIAH
)@@G@@NT, THE USER   *******  @H@@@!. ******* SPECIFIES A SET OF CHARACTER STRAI
)@@G@@INGS WHICH THE PROGRAM     *******  @H@@@!. ******* WILL COMPARE AGAINSTAJ
)@@G@@ HEADING IMAGES IN FILE.  IF A MATCH   *******  @H@@@!. ******* IS FOUNDAK
)@@G@@, THE FOLLOWING DATA IMAGES WILL BE PRINTED UNTIL  *******  @H@@@!. ****AL
)@@G@@*** THE NEXT HEADING CONTROL IMAGE IS ENCOUNTERED.  MANY       *******  AM
)@@G@@@H@@@!. ******* STRINGS CAN BE SPECIFIED (ONE PER DATA CARD FOLLOWING   AN
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. ******* THE PROCESSOR CALL).  AS EACH STRING IS MATCAO
)@@G@@HED, IT IS     *******  @H@@@!. ******* REMOVED FROM FURTHER CONSIDERATIAP
)@@G@@ON (UNLESS 'R' OPTION IS   *******  @H@@@!. ******* SPECIFIED).         AQ
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@!. *******         AR
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@!. ****AS
)@@G@@*** CALLING SEQUENCE: @QUICKTPR[,OPTIONS] FILE.                *******  AT
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******                   HEAD-1                                AU
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******                   HEAD-2                    AV
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. *******                   ......        AW
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@!. *******                   HEAX
)@@G@@AD N                                   *******  @H@@@!. *******         AY
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@!. ****AZ
)@@G@@*** SEVERAL VARIATIONS IN THE INPUT STRINGS ARE RECOGNIZED:    *******  BA
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******                                                         BB
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. ******* XXXXXXXX->YYYYYYYY - RANGE OF HEADINGS (ALL BC
)@@G@@REPORTS        *******  @H@@@!. *******                      BETWEEN THEBD
)@@G@@ TWO HEADINGS ARE PRINTED) *******  @H@@@!. ******* ->YYYYYYYY         -BE
)@@G@@ ALL REPORTS FROM BEGINNING TO HEADING *******  @H@@@!. *******         BF
)@@G@@             ARE PRINTED                           *******  @H@@@!. ****BG
)@@G@@*** XXXXXXXX->         - ALL REPORTS FROM HEADING TO END ARE   *******  BH
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******                      PRINTED                            BI
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******                                             BJ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. ******* FOLLOWING OPTIONS ARE RECOGNIZEDBK
)@@G@@:                          *******  @H@@@!. *******                     BL
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@!. ******* 'L' - PRBM
)@@G@@INT ALL HEADINGS FROM TAPE                         *******  @H@@@!. ****BN
)@@G@@*** 'R' - ALLOW MORE THAN 1 P/O PER INPUT HEADING              *******  BO
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******                                                         BP
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. ******* TO LIST ALL HEADINGS IN AN SDF PRINT FILE, SBQ
)@@G@@PECIFY         *******  @H@@@!. ******* 'L' AND 'R' OPTIONS AND NO INPUTBR
)@@G@@ HEADINGS.                 *******  @H@@@!. *******                     BS
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@!. ******* USE IS MBT
)@@G@@ADE OF THE 1110 BYTESUB ROUTINES AND 1100/80       *******  @H@@@!. ****BU
)@@G@@*** INSTRUCTIONS.                                              *******  BV
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******                                                         BW
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. ******* REVISION SUMMARY:                           BX
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. ******* ----------------                BY
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@!. *******                     BZ
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@!. ******* 1R1  - FCA
)@@G@@IRST RELEASE                                       *******  @H@@@!. ****CB
)@@G@@*** 1R2  - IDONLY$                                             *******  CC
)@@G@@@H@@@!. ******* 1R3  - CORRECTION FOR SMALL HEADINGS                    CD
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******      - ADD 'L' OPTION                       CE
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. ******* 1R4  - CHECK FOR NULL CONTROL IMCF
)@@G@@AGE                        *******  @H@@@!. *******      - CONSOLE P/O ICG
)@@G@@F BATCH                                *******  @H@@@!. ******* 2R1  - RCH
)@@G@@E-WRITEN USING SIR$ AND BYTESUB                    *******  @H@@@!. ****CI
)@@G@@***      - CONVERTED TO MASM                                   ******   CJ
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******      - TEST FACILITY ADDED                              CK
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******      - 'R' OPTION ADDED                     CL
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. *******      - MULTI-REEL FACILITY ADDEDCM
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@!. ******* 2R2  - BLANK 2ND WORCN
)@@G@@D OF INPUT HEADINGS                    *******  @H@@@!. *******      - UCO
)@@G@@SE FINDFIELD SUBROUTINE                            *******  @H@@@!. ****CP
)@@G@@***      - USE 1100/80 INSTRUCTIONS                            *******  CQ
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******      - UPDATE TEST FACILITY                             CR
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. ******* 3R1  - HANDLE ASCII PRINT CONTROL IMAGES    CS
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. *******      - UPDATE TEST FACILITY     CT
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@!. *******      - USE BYTESUB 2CU
)@@G@@R2                                     *******  @H@@@!. *******      - GCV
)@@G@@ENERALIZE INPUT STRING LOGIC                       *******  @H@@@!. ****CW
)@@G@@***      - ADD INPUT STRING VARIATIONS                         *******  CX
)@@G@@@H@@@\. *******      - PROCESS ANY SDF FILE (EVEN IF NOT PRINT FILE)    CY
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******                                             CZ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. ****************************************DA
)@@G@@**********************************  @E@@@!$(1),ST   LIPROC$             DB
)@@G@@        . INVOKE 'LI' PROCS   @E@@@!          TEP       A5,(1*/('Z'-'L')DC
)@@G@@) . INIT 'L' OPTION KEY @ @@@!          S         A5,LOPT   @E@@@!      DD
)@@G@@    TEP       A5,(1*/('Z'-'R')) . INIT 'R' OPTION KEY @ @@@!          S DE
)@@G@@        A5,ROPT   @G@@@!          AN,U      A4,6              . CALCULATDF
)@@G@@E BATCH KEY = RUN TYPE-6@F@@@!          S         A4,BATCH          . BADG
)@@G@@TCH=0 FOR BATCH RUN     @F@@@!          LMJ       X11,PREPF$        . PRDH
)@@G@@OCESS INPUT PARAMETERS  @C@@@!          ERR$                        . ERDI
)@@G@@ROR   @G@@@!          TEST                        . INVOKE TEST FACILITYDJ
)@@G@@ IF @MASM,T @E@@@!          LMJ       X11,IDLINE$       . GENERATE SIGN-DK
)@@G@@ON    @C@@@!          PRINT$    IDBUFF,8          . PRINT IT@D@@@!      DL
)@@G@@    PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   @G@@@!          L,U     DM
)@@G@@  X1,IMAGE          . INITILIAZE PTRS FOR STRING INPUT@ @@@!          L,DN
)@@G@@U       X2,HDBUFF @ @@@!          L         X3,(1,0)  @E@@@!LOOP1     REDO
)@@G@@AD$     IMAGE,INIT        . READ NEXT STRING    @D@@@!          L,U     DP
)@@G@@  A3,0,A0           . WORD COUNT    @ @@@!          LXI       A0,A3     DQ
)@@G@@@ @@@!          LXM,U     A0,IMAGE  @A@@@!          A         A0,(0100,0DR
)@@G@@)     @ @@@!          TNZ       BATCH     @F@@@!          PRINT$        DS
)@@G@@              . ECHO INPUT STRING IF BATCH@G@@@!          MSI,U     A3,6DT
)@@G@@              . CONVERT WORD COUNT TO BYTE COUNT@G@@@!LOOP2     AN,U    DU
)@@G@@  A3,1              . CALCULATE ACTUAL BYTE COUNT     @G@@@!          LXDV
)@@G@@I       X1,A3             .   BY SUBTRACTING TRAILING BLANKS@ @@@!      DW
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,BGET  @ @@@!          TNE,U     A0,' '    @ @@@!      DX
)@@G@@    J         LOOP2     @G@@@!          L,U       A0,1,A3           . MODY
)@@G@@VE INPUT STRING TO HDBUFF     @^@@@!          LXI,U     X1,0@ @@@!      DZ
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,BMOVE @G@@@!          S,S2      A0,HEAD,X3        . STEA
)@@G@@ORE BYTE COUNT IN HEAD TABLE  @E@@@!          L         A1,X2           EB
)@@G@@  . GET STARTING BYTE # @ @@@!          SSL       A1,18     @E@@@!      EC
)@@G@@    S,S1      A1,HEAD,*X3       . STORE IN HEAD TABLE @F@@@!          A ED
)@@G@@        A1,A0             . UPDATE HDBUFF POINTER     @ @@@!          LXEE
)@@G@@I       X2,A1     @F@@@!          INC       NHEAD             . INCREMENEF
)@@G@@T HEAD TABLE COUNT@#@@@!          NOP     @E@@@!          S         X2,XEG
)@@G@@4             . SAVE HDBUFF PTR     @H@@@!          L,U       X2,ARROW  EH
)@@G@@        . SEARCH FOR AN ARROW IN INPUT (->)     @ @@@!          L,U     EI
)@@G@@  A1,1,A3   @^@@@!          L,U       A2,2@A@@@!          LMJ       X11,EJ
)@@G@@FINDFIELD   @F@,@!          J         CONT0A            . NONE FOUND, NOEK
)@@G@@RMAL CASE   @F@@@,          J         CONT2             . NONE FOUND, NOEL
)@@G@@RMAL CASE   @G@@@!          TZ        A0                . IS ARROW IN BEEM
)@@G@@GINNING OF STRING?@B@,@!          J         CONT0             . NO@B@@@,EN
)@@G@@          J         CONT1             . NO@D@@@!          L,T1      A0,HEO
)@@G@@EAD-1,X3      . YES, GET SC,NC@I@@@!          A,U       A0,0176         EP
)@@G@@  . INCREMENT SC BY 2 AND DECREMENT NC BY 2     @F@@@!          S,T2    EQ
)@@G@@  A0,HEAD-1,X3      . MOVE TO 2ND STRING DESCR  @F@@@!          SZ,T1   ER
)@@G@@  HEAD-1,X3         . ZERO 1ST STRING DESCR     @ @,@!          J       ES
)@@G@@  CONT0A    @ @@@,          J         CONT2     @G@,@!CONT0     S,S2    ET
)@@G@@  A0,HEAD-1,X3      . CHANGE BYTE COUNT FOR 1ST STRING@G@@@,CONT1     S,EU
)@@G@@S2      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . CHANGE BYTE COUNT FOR 1ST STRING@F@@@!      EV
)@@G@@    TE,U      A3,1,A0           . IS ARROW AT END OF STRING?@B@@@!      EW
)@@G@@    J         $+3               . NO@F@@@!          SNZ,T2    HEAD-1,X3 EX
)@@G@@        . SET 2ND STRING DESCR TO -0@ @,@!          J         CONT0A    EY
)@@G@@@ @@@,          J         CONT2     @F@@@!          A,S1      A0,HEAD-1,EZ
)@@G@@X3      . GENERATE STRING 2 DESCR   @^@@@!          A,U       A0,2@A@@@!FA
)@@G@@          S,S3      A0,HEAD-1,X3    @A@@@!          AN,S2     A3,HEAD-1,FB
)@@G@@X3    @^@@@!          AN,U      A3,1@A@@@!          S,S4      A3,HEAD-1,FC
)@@G@@X3    @E@,@!CONT0A    L         X2,X4             . RESTORE HDBUFF PTR  FD
)@@G@@@E@@@,CONT2     L         X2,X4             . RESTORE HDBUFF PTR  @F@@@!FE
)@@G@@          J         LOOP1             . PROCESS NEXT INPUT STRING @H@@@!FF
)@@G@@INIT      L,U       A0,FCT            . INITIALIZE PRINT FILE FOR READINFG
)@@G@@G     @ @@@!          LXI,U     X11,PIRCB$@A@@@!          LIJ       X11,FH
)@@G@@BSDFIO$     @D@@@!          J         ERR2              . READ ERROR    FI
)@@G@@@D@@@!          SZ        SWAP              . CLEAR SWAP KEY@E@@@!LOOP3 FJ
)@@G@@    L,U       A0,FCT            . READ NEXT SDF IMAGE @ @@@!          LXFK
)@@G@@I,U     X11,PIRCB$@ @@@!          LIJ       X11,BSDFI$@D@@@!          J FL
)@@G@@        ERR2              . READ ERROR    @D@@@!          J         END FM
)@@G@@              . END OF SDF    @E@@@!          L         A1,CONTROL      FN
)@@G@@  . GET CONTROL WORD    @F@@@!          JP        A1,DATA           . CHFO
)@@G@@ECK IF DATA CONTROL     @H@@@!          L,S1      A0,CONTROL        . NOFP
)@@G@@, WHAT KIND OF SDF CONTROL IS IT?   @E@@@!          TE,U      A0,050    FQ
)@@G@@        . IS IT SDF HEADER?   @B@,@!          J         CONT1           FR
)@@G@@  . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT3             . NO@B@1@\          L FS
)@@G@@        A0,(PF 1,NMESS4,MESS4)@G@\@!          L,H1      A0,CONTROL      FT
)@@G@@  . IS IMAGE THE SDF PRINT HEADER?  @G@@@\          L,H1      A1,CONTROLFU
)@@G@@        . IS IMAGE THE SDF PRINT HEADER?  @A@\@!          TE        A0,(FV
)@@G@@0501125)    @A@1@\          TE        A1,(0501125)    @A@@@1          TNFW
)@@G@@E       A1,(0501125)    @^@@@1          J         $+4 @F@\@!          J FX
)@@G@@        ERR1              . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEADER  @F@1@\          PRFY
)@@G@@INT$                      . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEADER  @F@@@1          PRFZ
)@@G@@INT$    MESS4,NMESS4      . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEADER  @ @@@1          J GA
)@@G@@        LOOP3     @F@@@!          TNZ       LOPT              . IF 'L' OGB
)@@G@@PTION, PRINT LABEL@ @@@!          J         LOOP3     @H@@@!          PRGC
)@@G@@INT$    LABEL,NLABEL,2    . 'PRINT FILE HAS FOLLOWING LABEL ...'  @F@@@!GD
)@@G@@          E$DIT     EPKT              . PRINT LABEL INFORMATION   @ @@@!GE
)@@G@@          E$MSG     RUNID     @ @@@!          E$FD1     IMAGE+3   @^@@@!GF
)@@G@@          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     USERID    @ @@@!      GG
)@@G@@    E$FD2     IMAGE+5   @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$GH
)@@G@@MSG     PARTNO    @A@@@!          E$DECV    CONTROL,,S4     @^@@@!      GI
)@@G@@    E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     INDEV     @ @@@!          E$GJ
)@@G@@FD1     IMAGE+2   @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG   GK
)@@G@@  FILEN     @ @@@!          E$FD2     IMAGE     @^@@@!          E$SKIP  GL
)@@G@@  2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     CREATE    @ @@@!          E$TIME    IMAGGM
)@@G@@E+4   @^@@@!          E$SKIP    1   @ @@@!          E$DAY3    IMAGE+4   GN
)@@G@@@D@@@!          E$PRINT   2                 . PRINT LABEL   @D@@@!      GO
)@@G@@    PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   @ @@@!          J       GP
)@@G@@  LOOP3     @D@,@!CONT1     TE,U      A0,060            . PRINT CONTROL?GQ
)@@G@@@D@@@,CONT3     TE,U      A0,060            . PRINT CONTROL?@ @@@!      GR
)@@G@@    J         LOOP3     @H@@@!          L,S2      A0,CONTROL        . GEGS
)@@G@@T # OF WDS IN PRINT CONTROL IMAGE   @H@@@!          JZ        A0,LOOP3  GT
)@@G@@        . IF NO DATA, FIND NEXT CONTROL IMAGE   @D@@@!          S       GU
)@@G@@  A0,NWDS           . SAVE # OF WDS @E@@@!          MSI,U     A0,6      GV
)@@G@@        . CONVERT TO CHARS    @C@@@!          S         A0,NCHAR        GW
)@@G@@  . SAVE    @D@@@!          L,S6      X3,CONTROL        . GET CODE TYPE GX
)@@G@@@E@@@!          S,H1      X3,BASCII         . STORE FOR BYTESUB   @ @@@!GY
)@@G@@          SZ        PRINT     @ @@@!          L,U       X1,IMAGE  @ @@@!GZ
)@@G@@          L,U       X2,PRINT  @ @@@!          L         R1,A0     @ @@@!HA
)@@G@@          L,U       R2,12     @E@@@!          LMJ       X11,GETSFIELD   HB
)@@G@@  . GET NEXT SUBFIELD   @E@@@!          J         LOOP3             . ALHC
)@@G@@L BLANK, SKIP     @A@@@!          L         A0,('H@@@@@')   @F@@@!      HD
)@@G@@    TNE       A0,PRINT          . HEADING PRINT CONTROL?    @C@,@!      HE
)@@G@@    J         CONT2             . YES     @C@@@,          J         CONTHF
)@@G@@4             . YES     @F@@@!          TNZ       KPRINT            . NOHG
)@@G@@, IS PRINT KEY SET?     @C@@@!          J         LOOP3             . NOHH
)@@G@@, SKIP@F@,@!          J         CONT5             . YES, SUBMIT PRINT COHI
)@@G@@NTROL @F@@@,          J         CONT9             . YES, SUBMIT PRINT COHJ
)@@G@@NTROL @F@,@!CONT2     L         A0,(PF -0,0,0)    . WAS A REPORT JUST PRHK
)@@G@@INTED?@F@@@,CONT4     L         A0,(PF -0,0,0)    . WAS A REPORT JUST PRHL
)@@G@@INTED?@ @@@!          TZ        KPRINT    @E@@@!          PRINT$        HM
)@@G@@              . YES, START NEW PAGE @E@@@!          SZ        KPRINT    HN
)@@G@@        . CLEAR PRINT KEY     @D@@@!          SZ        KHEAD           HO
)@@G@@  . CLEAR HEAD KEY@G@@@!          TNZ       LOPT              . IF 'L' OHP
)@@G@@PTION, PRINT HEADING    @ @,@!          J         CONT3     @ @@@,      HQ
)@@G@@    J         CONT5     @^@@@!          SZ        A0  @ @@@!          LXHR
)@@G@@I       A0,NWDS   @A@@@!          A         A0,(0100,IMAGE) @ @@@!      HS
)@@G@@    EX        EPRINT,X3 @F@,@!CONT3     TZ        PRINTALL          . ISHT
)@@G@@ PRINT ALL KEY SET?     @F@@@,CONT5     TZ        PRINTALL          . ISHU
)@@G@@ PRINT ALL KEY SET?     @F@@@!          J         MATCH             . YEHV
)@@G@@S, ALL HEADINGS MATCH   @H@@@!          L         X5,(1,0)          . COHW
)@@G@@MPARE EACH INPUT HEADING TO IMAGE   @ @@@!          L,U       X2,HDBUFF HX
)@@G@@@E@@@!LOOP4     TNZ       HEAD,X5           . SKIP ZEROED HEADINGS@ @@@!HY
)@@G@@          J         ELOOP4    @D@@@,          SP1       KHEAD           HZ
)@@G@@  . SET HEAD KEY  @G@@@!          TZ,S4     HEAD,X5           . NORMAL CIA
)@@G@@ASE (SINGLE HEADING)?   @B@,@!          J         CONT3A            . NOIB
)@@G@@@B@@@,          J         CONT6             . NO@E@@@!          L,T1    IC
)@@G@@  A1,HEAD,X5        . YES, LOOK FOR MATCH @ @@@!          LMJ       X10,ID
)@@G@@SLIDE @F@@@!          J         ELOOP4            . NO MATCH, TRY NEXT HIE
)@@G@@EADING@^@@@,          TNZ       ROPT@D@,@!          SP1       KPRINT    IF
)@@G@@        . SET PRINT KEY @D@,@!          SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLIG
)@@G@@EAR ENTRY   @G@@@,          SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLEAR ENTRY IFIH
)@@G@@ NOT 'R' OPTION   @ @@@!          J         MATCH     @D@,@!CONT3A    TZII
)@@G@@,T1     HEAD,X5           . ->XXXX CASE?  @D@@@,CONT6     TZ,T1     HEADIJ
)@@G@@,X5           . ->XXXX CASE?  @B@,@!          J         CONT3B          IK
)@@G@@  . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT7             . NO@E@,@!          SPIL
)@@G@@1       KPRINT            . YES, SET PRINT KEY  @F@,@!          L,T2    IM
)@@G@@  A1,HEAD,X5        . LOOK FOR MATCH ON STRING 2@G@@@,          L,T2    IN
)@@G@@  A1,HEAD,X5        . YES, LOOK FOR MATCH ON STRING 2 @ @@@!          LMIO
)@@G@@J       X10,SLIDE @F@@@!          J         MATCH             . NO MATCHIP
)@@G@@, KEEP PRINTING   @F@@@!          SZ        HEAD,X5           . MATCH FOIQ
)@@G@@UND, CLEAR ENTRY  @ @@@!          J         MATCH     @E@,@!CONT3B    L,IR
)@@G@@T1      A1,HEAD,X5        . COMPARE STRING 1    @E@@@,CONT7     L,T1    IS
)@@G@@  A1,HEAD,X5        . COMPARE STRING 1    @ @@@!          LMJ       X10,IT
)@@G@@SLIDE @F@@@!          J         ELOOP4            . NO MATCH, TRY NEXT HIU
)@@G@@EADING@E@@@!          TZ,T2     HEAD,X5           . MATCH, XX-> CASE?   IV
)@@G@@@B@,@!          J         CONT3C            . NO@B@@@,          J       IW
)@@G@@  CONT8             . NO@F@@@!          SP1       PRINTALL          . YEIX
)@@G@@S, SET PRINT ALL KEY    @D@@@!          SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLIY
)@@G@@EAR ENTRY   @ @@@!          J         MATCH     @G@,@!CONT3C    SP1     IZ
)@@G@@  KPRINT            . XXX->YYY CASE, SET PRINT KEY    @F@,@!          SZJA
)@@G@@,T1     HEAD,X5           . CLEAR STRING 1 PORTION    @H@@@,CONT8     SZJB
)@@G@@,T1     HEAD,X5           . XXX->YYY CASE, CLEAR STRING 1 PORTION @ @@@!JC
)@@G@@          J         MATCH     @F@@@!ELOOP4    TLEM      X5,NHEAD        JD
)@@G@@  . ANY INPUT HEADINGS LEFT?  @E@@@!          J         LOOP4           JE
)@@G@@  . YES, TRY NEXT ONE   @F@@@!          TNZ       ROPT              . IFJF
)@@G@@ 'R' OPTION, KEEP GOING @G@@@!          TZ        KHEAD             . WEJG
)@@G@@RE ANY HEADINGS ENCOUNTERED?  @F@@@!          J         LOOP3           JH
)@@G@@  . NO MORE HEADS, NO MATCH   @F@@@!          J         END             JI
)@@G@@  . NO, NOTHING MORE TO DO    @F@@@!MATCH     SP1       KPRINT          JJ
)@@G@@  . MATCH FOUND, SET PRINT KEY@E@@@!          TZ        BATCH           JK
)@@G@@  . IF RUN IS BATCH,    @G@,@!          J         CONT4             .   JL
)@@G@@PRINT HEADING BEING PROCESSED @G@@@,          J         CONT9           JM
)@@G@@  .   PRINT HEADING BEING PROCESSED @F@@@!          LXI       X1,A0     JN
)@@G@@        . MOVE HEADING TO MESSAGE   @A@@@!          L         X2,(13,MESJO
)@@G@@S3)   @ @@@!          L,S2      A0,HEAD,X5@ @@@!          LMJ       X11,JP
)@@G@@BMOVE @ @@@!          A,U       A0,13     @A@@@!          S,H1      A0,CJQ
)@@G@@OMPKT+1     @F@@@!          COM$P     COMPKT            . SEND MESSAGE TJR
)@@G@@O CONSOLE   @^@,@!CONT4     TNZ       ROPT@H@,@!          SZ        HEADJS
)@@G@@,X5           . CLEAR INPUT HEAD IF NOT 'R' OPTION    @F@,@!CONT5     LXJT
)@@G@@I       A0,NWDS           . SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL IMAGE@F@@@,CONT9     LXJU
)@@G@@I       A0,NWDS           . SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL IMAGE@ @@@!          LXJV
)@@G@@M,U     A0,IMAGE  @ @@@!          EX        EPRTCN,X3 @ @@@!          J JW
)@@G@@        LOOP3     @E@@@!DATA      TNZ       KPRINT            . IS PRINTJX
)@@G@@ KEY SET?   @C@@@!          J         LOOP3             . NO, SKIP@D@@@!JY
)@@G@@          L,T2      A0,CONTROL        . LINE SPACING  @^@@@!          LSJZ
)@@G@@SL      A0,6@D@@@!          A,S2      A0,CONTROL        . WORD COUNT    KA
)@@G@@@ @@@!          LSSL      A0,18     @E@@@!          LXM,U     A0,IMAGE  KB
)@@G@@        . DATA IMAGE LOCATION @D@@@!          L,S6      X3,CONTROL      KC
)@@G@@  . CODE TYPE     @E@@@!          EX        EPRINT,X3         . PRINT DAKD
)@@G@@TA IMAGE    @ @@@!          J         LOOP3     @E@@@!END       PRTCN$  KE
)@@G@@  NOHEAD,1          . TURN OFF HEADING    @E@@@!          PRINT$    MESSKF
)@@G@@1,NMESS1,-1   . PRINT END MESSAGE   @E@@@!          LMJ       X11,POSTPRKG
)@@G@@$       . CLOSE INPUT FILE    @#@@@!          ERR$    @G@@@!          L KH
)@@G@@        X5,(1,0)          . CHECK IF ANY LEFT OVER HEADINGS @ @@@!      KI
)@@G@@    L,U       X1,HDBUFF @ @@@!          L,U       X2,PRINT  @ @@@!      KJ
)@@G@@    SZ        KHEAD     @ @@@!          SZ        BASCII    @ @@@!LOOP5 KK
)@@G@@    TNZ       HEAD,X5   @ @@@!          J         ELOOP5    @F@@@!      KL
)@@G@@    TZ        KHEAD             . IS THIS FIRST HEADING?    @B@,@!      KM
)@@G@@    J         CONT6             . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT10    KN
)@@G@@        . NO@E@@@!          PRINT$    MESS2,NMESS2,2    . 'HEADINGS NOT KO
)@@G@@FOUND'@D@@@!          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   @G@,@!KP
)@@G@@CONT6     TNZ,T1    HEAD,X5           . IS HEADING OF FORM: ->XXXX ?    KQ
)@@G@@@G@@@,CONT10    TNZ,T1    HEAD,X5           . IS HEADING OF FORM: ->XXXXKR
)@@G@@ ?    @C@,@!          J         CONT7             . YES     @C@@@,      KS
)@@G@@    J         CONT11            . YES     @F@@@!          LXI,S1    X1,HKT
)@@G@@EAD,X5        . NO, GET STARTING CHAR #   @D@@@!          L,S2      A0,HKU
)@@G@@EAD,X5        . GET # OF CHARS@ @@@!          TZ,T2     HEAD,X5   @G@@@!KV
)@@G@@          A,S4      A0,HEAD,X5        . ADD # OF CHARS IN 2ND STRING    KW
)@@G@@@G@@@!          TZ,S4     HEAD,X5           . IS HEADING A SINGULAR STRIKX
)@@G@@NG?   @F@@@!          A,U       A0,2              . NO, ADD 2 CHARS FOR KY
)@@G@@'->'  @ @,@!          J         CONT8     @ @@@,          J         CONTKZ
)@@G@@12    @E@,@!CONT7     LXI,S3    X1,HEAD,X5        . GET STARTING CHAR # LA
)@@G@@@E@@@,CONT11    LXI,S3    X1,HEAD,X5        . GET STARTING CHAR # @D@@@!LB
)@@G@@          AN        X1,(2,0)          . BACKUP TO '->'@D@@@!          L,LC
)@@G@@S4      A0,HEAD,X5        . GET # OF CHARS@D@@@!          A,U       A0,2LD
)@@G@@              . ADD 2 FOR '->'@G@,@!CONT8     LMJ       X11,BMOVE       LE
)@@G@@  . MOVE STRING TO PRINT BUFFER     @G@@@,CONT12    LMJ       X11,BMOVE LF
)@@G@@        . MOVE STRING TO PRINT BUFFER     @G@@@!          S,H1      A0,PLG
)@@G@@SYMB+4        . STORE # OF CHAR IN SYMB$ PKT    @ @@@!          L,U     LH
)@@G@@  A0,PSYMB  @D@@@!          ER        SYMB$             . PRINT HEADING LI
)@@G@@@C@@@!          SP1       KHEAD             . SET KEY @ @@@!ELOOP5    TLLJ
)@@G@@EM      X5,NHEAD  @ @@@!          J         LOOP5     @C@@@!          EXLK
)@@G@@IT$                       . EXIT    @A@\@!ERR1      PRINT$    MESS4,NMESLL
)@@G@@S4    @#@\@!          EXIT$   @D@@@!ERR2      TE,U      A5,1            LM
)@@G@@  . WAS EOF READ? @E@@@!          J         ERR2A             . NO, OTHELN
)@@G@@R I/O ERROR @F@@@!          TZ        SWAP              . WAS TAPE JUST LO
)@@G@@SWAPPED?    @D@@@!          ERR$                        . YES, ERROR    LP
)@@G@@@E@@@!          IOW$      IOPKT             . READ NEXT RECORD    @ @@@!LQ
)@@G@@          L,S1      A0,IMAGE  @G@@@!          TE,U      A0,054          LR
)@@G@@  . IS IT AN END-OF-REEL RECORD?    @C@@@!          J         END       LS
)@@G@@        . NO, STOP@F@@@!          TSWAP$    IOPKT             . YES, SWALT
)@@G@@P TO NEXT REEL    @D@@@!          S         A0,SWAP           . SET SWAPLU
)@@G@@ KEY  @E@@@!          PRINT$    MESS6,NMESS6,2    . 'TAPE SWAPPED .....'LV
)@@G@@@E@@@!          J         INIT              . RE-INITIALIZE SIR$  @A@@@!LW
)@@G@@ERR2A     PRINT$    MESS5,NMESS5    @#@@@!          EXIT$   @H@@@!. ****LX
)@@G@@**********************************************************************  LY
)@@G@@@H@@@!. ******* SLIDE HEADING PAST PRINT CONTROL IMAGE SUBROUTINE       LZ

)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. ******* INPUT A1= 0,0,SC,NC             MB

)@@G@@**********************************************************  @E@@@!SLIDE ME

)@@G@@L       A2,30     @E@@@!          LXI,S1    X2,A1             . GET STARMG

)@@G@@,SC2,NC2,0,0@C@@@!. WHERE 'SC1' IS STARTING CHARACTER OF STRING 1 @C@@@!NB

)@@G@@TARTING CHARACTER OF STRING 2 @C@@@!.       'NC2' IS NUMBER OF CHARS IN ND
